    古今图书集成医部全录卷四百十五

    小儿唇口齿舌喉病门

    　　　　千金方 【唐　孙思邈】

    　　　　　鹅口

    　　凡小儿初出腹有鹅口者，其舌上有白屑如米；剧者，鼻中亦有之。此由儿在胞胎中受谷气盛故也，或妊娠时嗜糯米使之然。治之之法，以发缠着头，沾井花水撩拭之，三日如此，便脱去；如不脱，可煮栗荴汁令浓，以绵缠着头拭之。若春夏无栗荴，可煮栗木皮，如用井花水法。[1p]

    Collection of Medical Works from Ancient and Modern Times, Volume 415

    Children’s Diseases of the Lips, Mouth, Teeth, Tongue, and Throat

    Thousand Gold Prescriptions (Tang Dynasty, Sun Simiao)

    Oral Thrush

    If a young child exhibits oral thrush upon emerging from the womb, their tongue will have white flakes like rice; in severe cases, these flakes may also be found in the nose. This condition arises from excessive intake of dampness from grains while in the womb, or due to the mother's craving for glutinous rice during pregnancy. To treat it, cover the head with a cloth, dab it with well water, and clean it for three days; it should then clear up. If it doesn’t, boil the juice of the chestnut's inner skin until thick, and use a cloth to dab it. In spring and summer, if chestnut inner skin is not available, you can boil the bark of the chestnut tree, applying the same method with well water.[1p]

    　　　　　重舌

    　　小儿初出腹有连舌，舌下有膜如石榴子中隔，连其舌下后，令儿言语不发不转也。可以爪摘断之，微有血出无害；若血出不止，可烧发作灰末敷之，血便止也。
    　　　　　重腭重龂

    　　小儿出腹六七日后，其血气收敛成肉，则口舌喉颊里清净也。若喉里舌上有物，如芦箨盛水状者，若悬痈有胀起者，可以绵缠长针，留刃处如粟米许大，以针刺决之，令气泄，去青黄赤血汁也。一刺之止，消息一日，未消者来日又刺之，不过三刺自消尽。余小小未消，三刺亦止，自然得消也。有着舌下如此者名重舌，有着颊里及上腭如此者名重腭，有着齿龂上者名重龂，皆刺去血汁也。刺后用盐洗拭，急用如圣散，或一字散掺刷。[2p]

    Tongue with Membrane

    When a small child is born with a connected tongue, beneath the tongue there is a membrane resembling the partition of a pomegranate. This membrane connects the tongue underneath, preventing the child from speaking or moving the tongue. It can be clipped with nails, resulting in a small amount of bleeding which is not harmful; if the bleeding does not stop, it can be cauterized until it becomes ash and applied to stop the bleeding.

    Thick Palate and Gums

    When a child is six or seven days old, the blood and qi consolidate into flesh, and the mouth, tongue, throat, and cheeks become clear. If there is something in the throat or on the tongue that resembles a water-filled reed or if there are bulging abscesses, a long needle can be wrapped with cotton, with the blade left about the size of a grain of millet, to pierce it and release the qi, expelling the blue, yellow, or red blood fluid. After one puncture, if swelling remains, it can be punctured again the next day, not exceeding three punctures to completely eliminate it. If any small remnants remain, three punctures are also sufficient for them to dissipate naturally. The condition under the tongue is called "thick tongue," if it is found in the cheeks and hard palate, it is called "thick palate," and if it is found on the gums, it is called "thick gums." All of these should have their blood fluid punctured. After puncturing, rinse with salt and immediately apply a sacred powder or a fine powdered remedy.[2p]

    　　　　　齿病论

    　　凡齿龂宣露，多是疳(上匿下虫)及月蚀，以角蒿灰夜敷龂间使满，勿食油，不过二三日瘥。食油及干枣即发。所以患齿者，忌油干枣及桂心。每旦以一捻盐内口中，以温水含，揩齿及叩齿百遍，为之不绝，不过五日，口齿印牢密。凡人齿龂不能食果菜者，皆由齿根露也。为此盐汤揩齿叩齿法，无不愈也，神良。凡人好患齿病，多由月蚀夜食饮之所致也，识者深宜慎之。所以日月蚀未平时，特忌饮食。小儿亦然。[3p]

    Treatise on Tooth Diseases

    In general, the exposure of the gums is often due to deficiencies (with pests hidden above and below) and lunar eclipses. Apply the ash of the horsetail at night between the gums to fill the spaces; avoid eating oils, and within two or three days, it will heal. Consuming oils and dried jujubes will provoke the issue. Therefore, those suffering from dental problems should avoid oils, dried jujubes, and cassia bark. Every morning, take a pinch of salt in your mouth, swish with warm water, and rub and tap your teeth a hundred times; do this without fail, and within five days, the teeth will be firmly set. Generally, those who cannot eat fruits and vegetables have exposed tooth roots. This method of using saltwater to clean and tap the teeth is universally effective and excellent. The tendency to suffer from dental diseases often arises from eating or drinking during lunar eclipses, so knowledgeable individuals should be especially cautious. Thus, during lunar eclipses, one should strictly avoid food and drink. The same advice applies to children.[3p]

    　　　　小儿直诀 【宋　钱乙】

    　　　　　弄舌

    　　弄舌者，脾脏微热，令舌络牵紧，时时舒热，当少用泻黄散。或饮水者脾胃虚而津液少也，兼面黄肌瘦五心烦热者疳瘦也，用胡黄连丸。大病未已而弄舌者，凶。　　 【注　按小儿舌微露而即收，名弄舌，属心脾亏损，用温脾散补之。舌舒长而收缓舌吐舌，乃心脾积热，少用泻黄散主之。兼口舌生疮，作渴饮冷，属胃经实热，用泻黄散。作渴畏冷，属胃经虚热，用四君子汤。食少作渴，或大便不实，脾胃虚弱也，用七味白朮散。口角流涎，或腮颊患肿，胃虚风热也，先用人参安胃散，后用七味白朮散。若午后甚者，脾血虚也，四物汤多加参、朮、茯苓：未应用补中益气汤，及审相胜。其疳瘦证，当参诸疳门。】[4p]

    Treatment for Children: Playing with the Tongue

    Playing with the tongue indicates a slight heat in the spleen, causing the tongue's veins to become tight, necessitating frequent warmth and relaxation. One should minimize the use of Yellow Powder. If a child drinks water but has a weak spleen and stomach with reduced fluids, accompanied by a pale face, thin body, and irritability with heat in the five hearts, it indicates malnutrition; here, take Hu Huanglian pills. If the playing with the tongue occurs during a serious illness, it is ominous.

    Note: The term "playing with the tongue" refers to a tongue that slightly protrudes and then retracts, indicative of deficiency in the heart and spleen, which should be treated with a warming spleen powder. If the tongue is stretched out and slowly retracts while protruding, it suggests accumulated heat in the heart and spleen, for which Yellow Powder should be minimized. If there are sores on the mouth and tongue with thirst for cold drinks, it indicates excessive heat in the stomach channel, requiring Yellow Powder. If there is a thirst accompanied by aversion to cold, it signifies deficiency heat in the stomach channel, to be treated with the Four Gentlemen Decoction. If there is little food intake with thirst, or loose stools, indicating weakness in the spleen and stomach, use the Seven-Flavored Atractylodes Powder. If there is drooling from the corners of the mouth or swelling in the cheeks, it may indicate spleen deficiency with wind heat, initially using Ren Shen An Wei Powder, followed by the Seven-Flavored Atractylodes Powder. If symptoms are severe in the afternoon, it suggests deficiency of spleen blood, thus the Four Substances Decoction should include more ginseng, atractylodes, and poria. One should not use the Bu Zhong Yi Qi Decoction without first assessing compatibility. For malnutrition symptoms, refer to the relevant malnutrition guidelines.[4p]

    　　　　　舌厚唇燥

    　　急欲乳不能食者，此风邪由脐而蕴热心脾，至舌厚唇燥，不能吮乳也。　　 【注　按前证果因外邪而唇口撮紧者，是名为脐风，多不能救。若心脾有热，舌尖痛不能吮乳，舌本痛不能送乳者，以柳花散敷之。若舌下肿如小舌者，或舌络牵痛，或齿龈患白星，俱用线针刺出毒血，亦敷前散。若唇肿痛，或裂纹作痛，以当归膏调前散敷之。若暴病发热，作渴饮冷，大便秘结，用泻黄散疏导其热。若病后发热，口渴饮汤，大便不实，用异功散调补胃气。[5p]

    If one is urgently wanting to suckle but cannot due to a thick tongue and dry lips, it is a sign that wind pathogenic factors have accumulated heat in the heart and spleen, leading to this condition.

    Note: If the symptoms stem from external pathogens causing tightness in the lips and mouth, it is known as "navel wind," which is often difficult to treat. If there is heat in the heart and spleen, leading to pain at the tip of the tongue that prevents sucking, or pain affecting the base of the tongue that hinders milk flow, apply a powder of willow blossoms. If the underside of the tongue is swollen like a small tongue, or if there is pain due to tension in the tongue veins or problems with the gums presenting white spots, use a fine needle to draw out toxic blood, and also apply the aforementioned powder. If the lips are swollen and painful, or if there are painful cracks, mix angelica ointment with the powder for application. If a severe illness causes fever and thirst for cold drinks, along with constipation, use a purging formula to relieve the heat. If the illness has left one with a fever, thirst for soup, and loose stools, use a formula to nourish the stomach qi.[5p]

    若服攻伐之剂，兼呕吐或腹痛，脾胃复伤也，用四君子汤。或口角流涎，或痰气壅盛，脾不能摄也，用六君子汤。若儿自食甘肥，或母食酒面，致儿口舌生疮，用清胃散以清热。若作呕，少食泄泻，用白朮散以补脾。若手足并冷，或腹痛恶寒，用六君、炮姜以温中。若因乳母饮食劳役失宜，发热致儿，用补中益气汤。因乳母肝胆二经血虚，内热传儿，用加味逍遥散、八珍汤。因乳母肝脾郁怒，血伤内热，致儿为患，用加味逍遥散、加味归脾汤，俱加漏芦，子亦服数滴。仍须参前弄舌类详看。】[6p]

    If one takes a decoction for attacking and invading factors, along with vomiting or abdominal pain, it harms the spleen and stomach; use the Four Gentlemen Decoction. If there is drooling from the mouth or phlegm obstructing, indicating that the spleen cannot contain, use the Six Gentlemen Decoction. If a child eats sweet and fatty foods, or if the mother consumes wine or flour, resulting in sores on the child's mouth and tongue, use the Clear Stomach Powder to eliminate heat. If there are vomiting and reduced appetite with diarrhea, use the Atractylodes Powder to tonify the spleen. If the hands and feet are cold, or there is abdominal pain with aversion to cold, use the Six Gentlemen with roasted ginger to warm the middle. If a mother's improper diet and labor cause a fever in the child, use the Supplementing the Middle and Benefiting Qi Decoction. If the mother has blood deficiency in the liver and gallbladder, transferring internal heat to the child, use the Modified Free and Easy Wanderer Powder and Eight Treasure Decoction. If the mother experiences liver and spleen stagnation with anger, damaging blood and causing internal heat that harms the child, use the Modified Free and Easy Wanderer Powder and Modified Return the Spleen Decoction, both with added reed. The child may also take a few drops. It is necessary to refer back to previous details regarding tongue assessments.[6p]

    　　　　儒门事亲 【元　张从政】

    　　　　　口疮唇紧

    　　凡小儿口疮唇紧，用酸浆水洗去白痂，临困点绿袍散；如或不愈，贴赴筵散；又不愈，贴铅白霜散则愈。
    　　　　　牙疳

    　　牙疳者，齿龋也；齿龋者，牙龂腐烂也。下牙属手阳明大肠之经，燥金为主；上牙属足阳明胃经，湿土为主。上下是肠胃二经也。或积热于内，或因服银粉、巴豆大毒之药，入于肠胃，乳食不能胜其毒，毒气循经而至于齿龂牙缝嫩薄之分、反为害也。可以腐香玉线子治之。乳母临卧，当服黄连解毒汤一服，牙疳病则愈矣。
    　　　　平治会萃 【元　朱震亨】[7p]

    Caring for Parents in the Confucian Way
    By Zhang Congzheng

    Mouth Sores and Tight Lips

    For young children with mouth sores and tight lips, wash away the white crust with sour jujube water, and when in difficulty, sprinkle green robe powder. If it does not improve, apply banquet powder; if it still does not cure, then applying lead white powder will bring recovery.

    Tooth Rot

    Tooth rot refers to the decay of teeth; this decay is due to the rotting of the gums. The lower teeth correspond to the hand Yangming Large Intestine meridian, which is primarily associated with dryness and metal; the upper teeth correspond to the foot Yangming Stomach meridian, primarily associated with dampness and earth. Together, they are the two meridians of the intestines and stomach. If there is accumulated heat within, or due to the ingestion of toxic medicines like silver powder or large doses of croton, entering the intestines and stomach, milk and food cannot withstand the poison, leading the toxic qi to affect the gums and the delicate gaps between the teeth, causing harm. It can be treated with fragrant jade thread. When a wet nurse is about to sleep, she should take a dose of coptis detoxifying soup, and the tooth rot will be cured.[7p]

    　　　　　木舌

    　　戴云：木舌者，舌肿硬不和软也。又言重舌者，亦是此类。二者盖是热病，用百草霜、滑石、芒硝为末，酒调敷。
    　　　　　口糜

    　　戴云：谓满口生疮者便是。江茶、粉草敷之；或用苦参、黄丹、五倍子、青黛各等分敷之。
    　　　　世医得效方 【元　危亦林】

    　　　　　齿不生

    　　齿不生者，由齿者骨之所络，髓之所养；禀气不足则髓不能充于骨，故齿久不生。宜服芎黄散。
    　　　　奇效良方 【明　方贤】

    　　　　　弄舌

    　　夫弄舌者，脾脏微热，令舌络微紧，时时舒舌。治之切不可用凉药下之，少与龙脑饮子，地黄膏治之。若大病未已弄舌者凶，学者慎之。
    　　　　片玉心书 【明　万全】

    　　　　　唇疮

    　　儿疳(上匿下虫)，昏睡烦躁，鼻烂汁臭，齿龂七疮，下利黑血。虫食下部为狐，下唇有疮；虫食其脏为惑，上唇有疮。
    　　　　婴童百问 【明　鲁伯嗣】[8p]

    Wooden Tongue

    Dai Yun: Wooden tongue refers to a swollen and hard tongue that lacks the softness of a normal one. A heavy tongue also belongs to this category. Both conditions are generally due to heat illness. Use a powder made from a mix of various herbs like frost, talcum, and Glauber's salt, and apply it with wine.

    Mouth Ulcers

    Dai Yun: This refers to having sores throughout the mouth. Apply tea from the Jiang region and powdered herbs; alternatively, mix equal parts of苦参 (苦参),黄丹 (yellow orpiment),五倍子 (galla chinensis), and青黛 (indigo) for application.

    Effective Treatments by Contemporary Physicians (Yuan era, Wei Yilin)

    Teeth Not Growing

    The lack of tooth growth occurs because teeth are nourished by the bone and marrow. If the vital energy is insufficient, the marrow cannot nourish the bones, leading to prolonged absence of teeth. It is advisable to take Xiong Huang San.

    Remarkable Treatments (Ming era, Fang Xian)

    Playing with the Tongue

    Playing with the tongue indicates slight heat in the spleen, causing the tongue veins to become slightly tense; one should stretch the tongue from time to time. It is crucial not to use cooling medicines for treatment. A little bit of Long Nao Yin Zi and Di Huang Gao should be used. If the condition persists in a serious illness, it is ominous; practitioners should be cautious.

    Notes from the Heart (Ming era, Wan Quan)

    Lip Sores

    In children with intestinal worms, symptoms include drowsiness, irritability, a foul-smelling nose, gum sores, and black blood in diarrhea. Worms in the lower body cause sores on the lower lip, while those affecting the organs lead to sores on the upper lip.

    Hundred Questions about Infants (Ming era, Lu Boshi)[8p]

    　　　　　鹅口口疮

    　　巢氏曰：鹅口候者，小儿初生，口里白屑，满口上古，如鹅之口，故曰鹅口也。此乃胎热而心脾最盛，熏发于口也。葛氏用发缠指头，蘸井花水揩拭之；睡时以黄丹煅出火气，掺于舌上。小儿初出腹有连舌，舌下有膜，如石榴子中隔，连其舌下，后令儿言语不发不转也。可以爪甲摘断之，微有血出无害；若血出不止，可烧发作灰末傅之，血便止也。用保命散，枯白矾一钱，马牙硝半钱，朱砂一分，同研细，取白鹅粪以水搅取汁，调涂舌上颔颊内。先用发缠指揩拭舌上垢了，然后用药敷之。口疮候乃小儿血气盛，兼将养过温，心脏积热，熏蒸于上焦，故成口疮也。宜用南星末，淡酢调贴两脚心；乳母宜服洗心散，却用泻心汤。敷口之法，用黄连末以蜜水调抹口中。黄蘗、青黛、冰片皆可。又以牛黄少许末之，竹沥调涂口内，治鹅口。以马牙硝如豆许涂亦好。或口如鱼口不能合，或作鸦声者，难治。[9p]

    Candidiasis (Thrush)

    Chao Shi said: The condition called "candidiasis" refers to infants at birth who have white flakes in their mouths, filling their oral cavity like that of a goose, hence the name. This occurs due to heat from the fetus, with the heart and spleen being particularly vigorous, which manifests in the mouth. Ge Shi advised using hair wrapped around the finger to dip in well water and wipe the mouth; at night, burning yellow minerals to extract heat and applying it to the tongue. If the infant has a "fused tongue" with membrane underneath, similar to the partitions in a pomegranate, it may cause difficulty in speaking later on. One can cut it carefully, which may produce a little blood but is not harmful; if the bleeding does not stop, one can burn the hair to ash and apply it to stop the bleeding.

    Use the Baoming powder: one qian of dried white alum, half a qian of horse's tooth nitre, and one fen of vermilion, finely ground together. Take white goose droppings, mix it with water to extract juice, and apply it inside the mouth and on the cheeks. First, use the hair to clean off any filth on the tongue, then apply the medicine. The occurrence of mouth sores is due to the infant having an abundance of blood energy and being overly nourished, causing heat accumulation in the heart, which steams upward, resulting in mouth sores.

    One should use powdered southern star herb mixed with light vinegar and apply it to the soles of the feet; wet-nurses should take the Xixin powder while also taking the Xiexin Decoction. For treating the mouth, use powdered huanglian mixed with honey water to apply inside. Huangbo, qingdai, and ice shavings are all effective. Additionally, using a small amount of niuhuang powdered and bamboo juice applied inside the mouth can treat candidiasis. Applying horse's tooth nitre in a bean-sized amount is also good. If the mouth resembles a fish's and cannot close, or if it makes crowing sounds, it is difficult to treat.[9p]

    　　　　　重舌木舌弄舌

    　　巢氏曰：小儿重舌者，心脾俱有热也。心候于舌而主血，脾之络脉出于舌下。若心脾有热，则血气俱盛，附于舌根，重生壅出如舌而短小是也。有着颊里及上腭者，名曰重腭；着齿龈者，曰重龈。皆当刺去其血，用真蒲黄敷之；或发灰、或马牙硝、或硼砂、或焰硝敷之；或竹沥浸黄蘗点之，亦好。　　又木舌证，舌者心之候，脾之脉络于舌也。脏腑壅滞，心脾积热，热气上冲，故令舌肿，渐渐胀大，塞满口中，是为木舌。若不急疗，必致害人。[10p]

    The Nest Family said: Children with a heavy tongue have heat in both the heart and spleen. The heart is represented by the tongue and governs the blood, while the meridians of the spleen emerge from under the tongue. When there is heat in both the heart and spleen, the blood and qi become abundant, accumulating at the root of the tongue, causing it to appear heavy, thickened, and short. If it affects the inner cheeks and upper palate, it is called a heavy palate; if it affects the gums, it is called heavy gums. In all cases, one should eliminate the blood by needling and apply true cattail pollen; alternative treatments include applying ash, horse’s tooth nitrate, borax, or alchemical nitrate; or using bamboo juice mixed with berberine for application, which is also effective.

    Additionally, the condition referred to as a "wooden tongue" occurs when the tongue indicates the state of the heart and the meridians of the spleen are obstructed. With the internal organs stagnant, heat accumulates in the heart and spleen, leading the heat to surge upward and causing the tongue to swell, gradually enlarging and filling the mouth, resulting in a wooden tongue. If not treated urgently, it will surely cause harm.[10p]

    用(石卜)硝二分，紫霜一分，白盐半分，同研，每半钱竹沥井花水调敷。不用(石卜)硝及盐亦可。又方，用黄葵花研细，竟丹半之，同研点七次。又舌胀满口，单用冰片点之亦妙。　　又弄舌者，脾脏微热，令舌络微紧，时时舒舌。治之勿用冷药下之，当少与泻黄散渐服之。亦或饮水，医疑为热，必以冷药下之，非也。饮水者，脾胃虚，津液少也。又加面黄肌瘦，五心烦热，即为疳瘦，宜胡黄连丸辈。大病未愈，用药后弄舌者，凶。又有舌上白胎并黑色者，用硼砂为末掺之；热甚者加冰片，或单用黄丹如豆许，以按舌下尤妙。
    　　　　　齿迟[11p]

    Use two parts of stone nitrate, one part of purple frost, and half a part of white salt, grind them together, and mix them with half a cash of bamboo juice and well water for application. It is also acceptable not to use stone nitrate and salt. Another method involves finely grinding yellow hibiscus flowers, using half the amount of cinnabar, and grinding them together seven times for application. If the tongue swells and fills the mouth, applying just borneol is also effective.

    Furthermore, if there is tongue movement, it indicates slight heat in the spleen, causing the tongue veins to tighten. One should relax the tongue regularly. When treating this, do not use cold medicines; instead, gradually administer yellow powder. If water consumption is suspected to be heat-related, do not use cold medicines, as this is misleading. Drinking water indicates spleen and stomach deficiency, with a lack of fluids. Additionally, if the complexion is pale and thin, accompanied by five hearts feeling hot, it indicates malnutrition and should be treated with substances like hu huanglian pills.

    If the illness is severe and there is tongue movement after medication, it is a bad sign. For a white coating on the tongue accompanied by black spots, powder borax and mix it; if heat is severe, add borneol or simply use yellow lead the size of a bean to press under the tongue, which is particularly effective.
    Teeth are slow to grow.[11p]

    　　聂氏云：禀受肾气不足者，即髓不强。盖骨之所络而为髓，髓不足故不能充于齿，所以齿生迟也。宜用芎藭、干地黄、山药、当归、芍药、甘草各等分研末，用熟水调服，或时以药末擦牙龈，齿即生也。
    　　　　　喉痹腮肿

    　　巢氏云：此二证乃风毒之气客于咽喉，与血气相搏而结肿成毒，热入于心，即烦乱不食而死。此候急用金星丸下之。治小儿咽喉腮肿疼痛，当用升麻、马牙硝、硼砂、牛黄等剂，连翘汤不可缺也，连翘漏芦汤亦可服。
    　　　　　滞颐

    　　巢氏云：小儿滞颐者，涎流出而渍于颐间也。此由脾冷涎多故也。脾之液为涎，脾胃虚冷，不能收制其津液，故流出渍于颐也。张氏温脾丹主之。一法百药煎含咽，其涎自不出，亦截法也。益黄散亦治此证，温脾散亦可服。
    　　　　医学正传 【明　虞抟】

    　　　　　重舌重龈

    　　儿有重舌、重龈者，宜用三棱针刺去血，内服东垣凉膈散。凡口内诸病，惟针最捷。[12p]

    Nie said: "Those who inherit insufficient kidney qi will have weak marrow. Since the marrow is what nourishes the bones, if the marrow is insufficient, it cannot reach the teeth, which is why tooth development is delayed. One should take equal parts of Chuanxiong, Gan Di Huang, Shan Yao, Dang Gui, Shao Yao, and Gan Cao, grind them into a powder, and take with warm water. Alternatively, one can rub the gum with the powdered medicine, and the teeth will grow."

    Throat Blockage and Swelling of the Cheeks

    Chao said: "These two conditions are due to wind and poison qi affecting the throat, which combines with blood qi to form a swelling that becomes toxic. If heat enters the heart, it will lead to agitation, lack of appetite, and potentially death. For this condition, one should urgently administer Jin Xing Wan. For children with throat and cheek swelling and pain, one should use Sheng Ma, Ma Ya Xie, Borax, and Niu Huang, and Lian Qiao Decoction is essential; Lian Qiao and Lu Decoction can also be taken."

    Stagnation in the Jaw

    Chao said: "When children have stagnation in the jaw, saliva flows out and accumulates in the jaw area. This is due to a cold spleen leading to excessive saliva. The liquid of the spleen is saliva, and when the spleen and stomach are deficient and cold, they cannot control the secretion of fluids, causing the saliva to flow out and accumulate in the jaw. Zhang's Wen Pi Dan can treat this. Another method is to use a combination of various herbs for decoction and hold them in the mouth; this will also prevent saliva from flowing out. Yi Huang San can also treat this condition, and Wen Pi San can be taken as well."

    Medical Principles by Yu Tuan

    Heavy Tongue and Gums

    For children with heavy tongues and gums, it is advisable to use a three-edged needle to draw blood and internally take Dong Yuan Liang Ge San. Overall, for any oral issues, acupuncture is the most efficient.[12p]

    　　　　身经通考方 【明　吴昆】

    　　　　　舌肿

    　　小儿噤风，凡舌肿下必有噤虫，状如蝼蛄，有头毛，其头小白，可烧铁烙头上即消；不急治能杀人。世传走马喉痹，满口白疮如雪，脾虚所致。若带风邪，当先泻其邪，进补脾气生脾血之剂。盖龙火不宜凉物，宜以甘温从治也。
    　　　　保婴撮要 【明　薛铠】

    　　　　　滞颐

    　　小儿滞颐者，涎流出而渍于颐间也。脾之液为涎，由脾胃虚寒不能收摄耳。治用六君子汤加木香。凡作渴饮冷者，属实热，宜泻胃火；作渴饮汤者，属虚热，宜补中益气。若脾经实热，而廉泉不能约制者，用牛黄清心丸；脾经虚热而廉泉不能统摄者，用六君子加木香。胃经实热而虫动，津液流出者，用泻黄散；处热，用五味异功散。大便秘结，用清凉饮；中气下陷，用补中益气汤；食积内热，用大安丸。仍参口疮腮肿条互览之。[13p]

    Swollen Tongue

    For children with wind-stopping, if the tongue is swollen, there must be a “stopping worm” present, resembling a mole cricket, with fine hair on its head, which is small and white. Burning it with a heated iron can make it disappear; if not treated urgently, it can be fatal. It is said that a horse may cause throat paralysis, with the mouth full of white sores like snow, resulting from spleen deficiency. If influenced by wind evil, one should first dispel the evil and then take tonics to nourish the spleen qi and generate spleen blood. Dragon fire does not suit cooling substances; it is advisable to treat it with sweet and warm remedies.

    Stagnant Saliva

    For children with stagnant saliva, drooling occurs and seeps into the jaw area. The liquid of the spleen is saliva, which cannot be contained due to the cold deficiency of the spleen and stomach. The treatment is to use the Six Gentlemen Decoction with added patchouli. If the child is thirsty and drinks cold, it pertains to excess heat, hence, one should clear the stomach fire; if thirsty and drinking soup, it indicates deficiency heat, needing supplementation of the Middle and enhancement of qi. If there is excess heat in the spleen channel and the submandibular gland cannot regulate, use Niuhuang Qingxin Wan; if there is deficiency heat in the spleen channel, use Six Gentlemen with patchouli. For excess heat in the stomach channel causing worms to stir and fluids to flow out, use Xie Huang Powder; for heat, use Five Flavor Different Effect Powder. For constipation, use a cooling drink; for sinking middle qi, use Bu Zhong Yi Qi Decoction; if there is food accumulation and internal heat, use Da An Wan. Additionally, refer to the sections on mouth sores and swelling for further guidance.[13p]

    　　　　　喉痹

    　　小儿喉痹，因膏梁积热，或禀赋有热，或乳母七情之火，饮食之毒，当分其邪蓄表里，与证之轻重，经之所主而治之。若左腮色青赤者，肝胆经风热也，用柴胡栀子散。右腮色赤者，肺经有热也，用泻白散。额间色赤者，心与小肠经热也，用导赤散；若兼青色，风热相搏也，用加味逍遥散。鼻间色黄，脾胃经有执也，用泻黄散；若兼青色，木乘土位也，用加味逍遥散；兼赤色，心传土位也，用柴胡栀子散。颏间色赤，肾经有热也，用地黄丸。凡此积热内蕴，二便不通者，当疏利之；风邪外客而发寒热者，当发散之；外感风邪，大便闭结，烦渴痰盛者，当内疏外解。若因乳母膏梁积热者，母服东垣清胃散；若因乳母恚怒肝火者，母服加味逍遥散。禀赋阴虚者，儿服地黄丸。大概当用轻和之剂以治其本，切不可用峻利之药以伤真气也。[14p]

    Throat Obstruction

    In children, throat obstruction occurs due to accumulated heat from rich foods, or due to inherent heat, or from the negative emotions of the wet nurse, or from toxic food and drink. It is important to differentiate the nature of the obstruction and its severity, and to treat according to the respective meridian it pertains to. If the left cheek appears bluish-red, it is due to wind-heat in the liver and gallbladder meridians; treat with Chai Hu and Zhi Zi powder. If the right cheek is red, there is heat in the lung meridian; treat with Xie Bai powder. If the forehead is red, it indicates heat in the heart and small intestine meridians; use Dao Chi powder. If there is also a bluish tint, it suggests a combination of wind and heat, and treat with a modified Xiao Yao powder. If there is a yellow color between the nostrils, it indicates obstruction in the spleen and stomach meridians; treat with Xie Huang powder. If there is also a bluish color, it implies wood overcoming earth; use modified Xiao Yao powder. If red, it indicates the heart's influence over the earth; treat with Chai Hu and Zhi Zi powder. If there is redness on the chin, it suggests heat in the kidney meridian; use Di Huang pills. In cases where there is accumulated heat internally and difficulty with urination and defecation, the treatment should alleviate and open these pathways. If there is an external wind pathogen causing chills and fever, it should be expelled. If wind pathogen is present along with constipation and excessive thirst and phlegm, internal release and external resolution are needed. If the obstruction is due to heat accumulated from the wet nurse's rich diet, the mother should take Dong Yuan's Clear Stomach powder; if caused by her anger and liver fire, she should take modified Xiao Yao powder. If the child is constitutionally yin deficient, they should take Di Huang pills. Generally, mild and harmonious medications should be used to treat the underlying condition, avoiding harsh and damaging drugs that harm the vital energy.[14p]

    　　　　　吐舌弄舌

    　　舌属心脾二经。小儿舌微露而即收者，名弄舌，此属心脾亏损，用温脾散补之。舌舒长而良久不收者，名吐舌，乃心脾积热，用泻黄散主之。或兼口舌生疮，作渴饮冷，属胃经实热，亦用前散。作渴饮热，属胃经虚热，用四君子汤。食少作渴，或大便不实，脾胃虚弱也，用七味白朮散。口角流涎，或腮颊患肿，胃虚风热也，先用人参安胃散，次用七味白朮散。若午后甚者，脾血虚也，四物多加参、朮、茯苓；未应，用补中益气汤，及审五脏相胜。若因疳瘦所致，当参诸疳门。
    　　　　古今医统 【明　徐春甫】

    　　　　　口疮

    　　口疮者，乃脾气凝滞，风热加之，则发口疮。小儿将养太过温暖，心脏客热，其口亦疮。伤寒狐惑之证，上唇生疮，虫食其脏；下唇生疮，虫食其肛。此口疮内应脏腑之邪热然也。[15p]

    Tongue Play and Tongue Projection

    The tongue is associated with the heart and spleen meridians. When a child’s tongue slightly shows and then retracts immediately, it is called tongue play, indicating deficiency of the heart and spleen, to be treated with warming spleen powders. When the tongue extends and remains out for a long time, it is called tongue projection, which signifies accumulation of heat in the heart and spleen, to be addressed with purging yellow powders. If accompanied by sores in the mouth and thirst for cold drinks, this belongs to excess heat in the stomach meridian, and the same powders are used. If there is thirst for warm beverages, it indicates deficiency heat in the stomach meridian, to be treated with Four Gentlemen Decoction. If there is little food intake leading to thirst, or loose stools, it reflects weakness of the spleen and stomach, requiring Seven Flavor White Atractylodes Powder. If there is salivation at the corners of the mouth or swelling in the cheeks, it indicates wind-heat in a weak stomach; first, use Ginseng to Calm the Stomach Powder, then apply Seven Flavor White Atractylodes Powder. If the condition is severe in the afternoon, it suggests blood deficiency in the spleen; add more ginseng, atractylodes, and poria to the Four Substances Decoction. If it occurs due to malnutrition, reference should be made to the guidelines for malnourishment.

    Mouth Ulcers

    Mouth ulcers arise from stagnation of spleen qi, exacerbated by wind-heat, leading to their appearance. Children who are overly warmed and nourished may also have sores due to heat in the heart. In cases of febrile diseases, sores appearing on the upper lip indicate internal evil heat affecting the organs; sores on the lower lip signify internal heat harming the anus. These mouth ulcers are indeed connected to the evil heat from the internal organs.[15p]

    　　　　证治准绳 【明　王肯堂】

    　　　　　口

    　　婴儿新产出胎，急以绵裹指，揩拭儿口中舌上恶血秽露，谓之玉衔。若啼声一发，即入腹成百病。
    　　　　　舌

    　　又看舌下，若连舌有膜如石榴子。若啼不出、声不转，连以指爪摘断之，或用苇刀子割之。微有血出即活。若舌下血出多者，以烧乱发灰同猪脂少许和涂之。
    　　　　　齿唇

    　　《圣惠》云：看齿根有黄筋两条，以苇刀割断，点猪乳佳。如儿目难开，先点猪乳。　　儿上唇与齿龈连处，皆有一筋牵引。若上唇筋紧，即生上炼；下唇筋紧，即生下炼。上炼生疮，满头或眉间，如癣状。瘙痒不已，复流黄汁，至处生疮。下炼起腰背，渐至四肢，患亦如上。或疾甚不治，或头面上下相通，累年不愈，遂致夭折，或成大病。惟每日早晨拭口佳。[16p]

    Evidence and Treatment Criteria

    Mouth

    When an infant is newly born, it is urgent to wrap it in soft cloth and wipe away the foul blood and impurities from its mouth and tongue, referred to as "jade clasped." If the infant cries out, it will lead to various ailments.

    Tongue

    Next, examine under the tongue. If there is a membrane connecting the tongue like a pomegranate seed, and if the child does not cry or there is no change in voice, use your fingernail to cut it or use a reed knife to slice it. A slight amount of blood indicates vitality. If there is a significant amount of blood underneath the tongue, mix burnt fine ashes with a little pig fat and apply it.

    Teeth and Lips

    The "Holy Benefit" states: Observe the roots of the teeth; if there are two yellow veins, use a reed knife to sever them and apply pig's milk. If the child's eyes are hard to open, first apply pig's milk. The upper lip is connected to the gums by a vein. If the vein connecting the upper lip is tight, it causes conditions in the upper region; if the vein for the lower lip is tight, it leads to conditions in the lower region. Conditions in the upper part can result in sores that appear on the head or between the brows, resembling scabs. If itching persists and yellow fluid seeps out, sores will develop. Conditions arising from the lower part can affect the waist and back, eventually reaching the limbs, manifesting similarly as above. If severe cases are untreated, or if symptoms affect both head and face, it may lead to prolonged illness or even death. Daily morning mouth wiping is recommended.[16p]

    　　　　　口舌疮

    　　诸疳口疮，因乳哺失节，或母食膏梁积热，或乳母七情郁火所致。其证口舌齿龈，如生疮状。若发热作渴饮冷，额间色赤，左寸脉洪数者，此属心经，先用导赤散清心火，次用地黄丸滋肾水。若寒热作渴，左颊青赤，左关脉弦洪者，属肝经，先用柴胡栀子散清肝火，次用六味地黄丸生肝血。若两腮黄赤，牙龈腐拦，大便酸臭，右关脉洪数，按之则缓者，属脾经，用四味肥儿丸治脾火，以五味异功散补脾气。若发热咳嗽，右腮色赤，右寸脉洪数，按之濇者，属肺经，先用清肺饮治肺火，用五味异功散补脾胃。若发热作渴，两颊黧色，左尺脉数者，属肾经不足，先用六味地黄丸以生肾水，次用补中益气汤以生肺气。又有走马疳者，因病后脾胃气血伤损，虚火上炎，或痘疹余毒上攻，其患甚速，急用铜绿散、大芜荑汤。轻则牙龈腐烂，唇吻腮肿；重则牙龈蚀露，颊腮透烂。[17p]

    Mouth and Tongue Ulcers

    Mouth ulcers in children occur due to irregular breastfeeding, or from the mother consuming rich foods that generate heat, or from the emotions of the wet nurse causing fire. The symptoms appear on the lips, tongue, and gums resembling ulcers. If there is fever and thirst with a desire for cold drinks, a red complexion on the forehead, and a rapid left pulse, this indicates a heart issue. First, use Daohong San to clear heart fire, then use Di Huang Wan to nourish kidney water. If there are alternating chills and fever, with a blue-red left cheek and a taut and rapid left pulse, this relates to the liver channel. First, use Chai Hu Zhi Zi San to clear liver fire, then use Liu Wei Di Huang Wan to nourish liver blood. If both cheeks are yellow-red, the gums are decaying, the stool has a sour smell, and the right pulse is rapid yet soft, it indicates a spleen issue. Use Si Wei Fei Er Wan to treat spleen fire, and Wu Wei Yi Gong San to tonify spleen qi. If there is fever and coughing, with a red right cheek and a rapid right pulse that feels thin on palpation, this indicates a lung issue. First, use Qing Fei Yin to treat lung fire, and Wu Wei Yi Gong San to nourish the spleen and stomach. If there is fever and thirst, both cheeks are dark, and the left pulse is rapid, it shows deficiency in the kidney channel. First, use Liu Wei Di Huang Wan to produce kidney water, then use Bu Zhong Yi Qi Tang to generate lung qi.

    There is also a condition called "running horse dampness," which arises from damage to the spleen and stomach qi and blood after illness, leading to deficiency fire rising, or due to residual poison from measles attacking upward. The disease progresses rapidly and requires urgent use of Tonglu San and Da Wu Yi Tang. In mild cases, this leads to rotten gums and swollen lips and cheeks; in severe cases, the gums erode, and the cheeks and jaws become extensively decayed.[17p]

    若饮食不入，喘促痰甚，此脾胃虚而肺气败也；顿腮赤腐不知痛者，此胃气虚甚而肉死也，并不治。　　经云：手少阴之经通于舌，足太阴之经通于口。因心脾二经有热，则口舌生疮也。当察面图部位，分经络虚实而药之。若元气无亏，暴病口生白屑，或重舌者，用乱发缠指，蘸井花水揩之；或刺出毒血，以柳花散敷之。或上腭肿胀，或有泡者，并令刺破，敷前散，或以青黛搽之；刺后又生，又刺。[18p]

    If food and drink do not enter, and there is severe wheezing and phlegm, this indicates a deficiency in the spleen and stomach, leading to failure of lung qi; if there is a swollen cheek that is red and rotten without pain, this indicates a severe deficiency of stomach qi, resulting in dead tissue and should not be treated.

    The classics state: the Hand Shaoyin channel connects to the tongue, while the Foot Taiyin channel connects to the mouth. When there is heat in the heart and spleen channels, sores can appear on the mouth and tongue. One should examine the facial features and assess the deficiency or excess of the meridians for treatment.

    If the vital energy is not depleted and a sudden illness causes white spots in the mouth or a heavy tongue, one can use tangled hair to wrap around the fingers and dip it in well water to wipe it; or draw out toxic blood using needles and apply willow flower powder. If there is swelling in the palate or blisters, they should be punctured, with powder applied afterwards, or blue indigo can be used to rub on the area; if it recurs after needling, needle again.[18p]

    若唇吻坼裂者，用当归膏调柳花散敷之。若元气亏损或服寒凉之药，或兼作呕少食者，此虚热也，用五味异功散加升麻、柴胡；若泄泻作渴者，脾胃虚弱也，用七味白朮散；若腹痛恶寒者，脾胃虚寒也，用六君、姜、桂；若因母食酒面煎煿者，用清胃散；若因母饮食劳役者，用补中益气汤；肝脾血虚者，用加味逍遥散；郁怒内热者，用加味归脾汤，母子并服。若泥用降火，必变慢脾风矣。仍参吐舌弄舌治之。凡针重舌以线针直刺，不可横挑，恐伤舌络，致言语不清也。[19p]

    If the lips are cracked, apply a mixture of angelica ointment with willow flower powder. If there is a deficiency of vital energy or if cold medicines have been taken, or if there is nausea and poor appetite, this indicates a deficiency heat; use Wuwei Yigong powder with added Shengma and Chaihu. If there is diarrhea and thirst, it suggests weakness of the spleen and stomach; use Qiwwei Baizhu powder. If there is abdominal pain and aversion to cold, this points to cold deficiency of the spleen and stomach; use Liu Jun pill with ginger and cinnamon. If the mother’s food and drink were improperly prepared, use Qingwei powder. If the mother was overworked due to food and labor, use Buzhong Yiqi decoction. For liver and spleen blood deficiency, use Jiawei Xiaoyao powder. For internal heat due to frustration or anger, use Jiawei Guipi decoction, for both mother and child to take together. If there is mud (excess heat), it will inevitably change to slow wind of the spleen. Continue to apply treatments that involve sticking out and manipulating the tongue. When using needles on the tongue, it is better to insert them straight with a thin needle rather than piercing sideways, as this could damage the tongue's vessels and lead to unclear speech.[19p]

    　　　　　舌

    　　舌者心之候，脾之脉络于舌也。二经存热无所泄而发于舌，如舌络微紧，时时舒舌，谓之弄舌；附舌下近舌根，生形如舌而小，谓之重舌；舌惭渐肿大，塞满口中，谓之木舌。　　曾氏云：凡患此证，是脾与心肝屡受极热，所谓重舌木舌，又谓之舌黄鹅口，名虽异，皆热也。大抵重舌生于舌下，挺露如舌，故曰重舌。然脾之络脉系舌傍，肝之络脉系舌本，心之络脉系舌根。凡此三经或为湿热风寒所中，则舌卷缩、或舒长、或肿满，宜消黄散、绿袍散主之，及当归散、羌活散与服。[20p]

    The Tongue

    The tongue is a messenger of the heart and a channel of the spleen. When the two meridians retain heat without being released, it manifests in the tongue. If the tongue's veins feel slightly tense and one relaxes the tongue frequently, it is called "playing with the tongue." If there is a growth underneath the tongue close to the root that resembles a small tongue, it is referred to as "heavy tongue." If the tongue swells and fills the mouth, it is known as "wood tongue."

    The Zeng family states that all conditions related to this are due to the spleen, heart, and liver having been subjected to extreme heat, which is what is referred to as "heavy tongue" and "wood tongue." They are also called "yellow tongue" and "duck's mouth." Although the names differ, they all signify heat. Generally, the heavy tongue appears beneath the tongue, protruding like a tongue, hence it is called "heavy tongue." The spleen's channels are linked to the side of the tongue, the liver's channels connect to the base of the tongue, and the heart's channels are linked to the root of the tongue.

    If these three meridians are affected by damp heat or wind-cold, the tongue may curl, retract, stretch, or swell. It would be appropriate to use "Xiao Huang San" and "Lu Pao San" as treatments, along with "Dang Gui San" and "Qiang Huo San" to administer.[20p]

    　　　　　弄舌

    　　弄舌者，脾脏微热。田氏云：若肥实者，用牛黄散治之。
    　　　　　重舌

    　　田氏云：重舌治法，用苦竹沥渍黄蘗末，点舌上；如不愈，后用真蒲黄敷之，不过三次愈。用真蒲黄微炒，纸铺地上，出火气，研细，每挑些掺舌下，更以温水蘸熟帛，裹指轻按之，按罢掺药。
    　　　　　木舌

    　　曾氏云：木舌者，舌肿硬而妨乳食，此为风热盛也。以当归散、泻黄散、玉露饮皆可服之，次消黄散点擦舌上。盖舌者心之官，心热则生疮破裂，肝壅则血出如涌，脾闭则自胎如雪，热则肿满，风则强木，口合不开，四肢壮热，气喘语塞，即其候也。治法凉解上焦及心肝脾三经邪热，疏风化痰。初用百解散加五和汤，水姜灯心煎；次投以牛蒡汤同当归散，入生地黄，水姜煎服。[21p]

    Tongue Disturbances

    Tongue disturbances indicate a mild heat in the spleen. Tian says: If it is plump and solid, treat it with Niu Huang San.

    Heavy Tongue

    Tian says: For the treatment of a heavy tongue, use bitter bamboo juice to soak yellow bile powder and apply it to the tongue. If it does not improve, later use true pu huang to dress it; it will heal in no more than three applications. Lightly fry true pu huang, spread it on paper, release the heat, grind it finely, and use some to apply to the tongue. Then take warm water, dip a fine cloth, wrap your finger, and gently press it down; after pressing, apply the medicine.

    Wooden Tongue

    Zeng says: A wooden tongue is swollen and hard, hindering milk and food intake, indicating excessive wind-heat. Remedies such as Dang Gui San, Xie Huang San, and Yu Lu Yin can be taken; then apply Xie Huang San to rub on the tongue. The tongue is the organ of the heart; if the heart is heated, it will cause ulcers and cracks; if the liver is congested, blood will surge out; if the spleen is obstructed, it will be like snow from the fetus; if hot, it will swell; if windy, it will be strong and wooden, making the mouth close and difficult to open, limbs will feel strong heat, and there will be wheezing and speech difficulties—these are the signs. The treatment method involves cooling and resolving the upper jiao and the evil heat in the heart, liver, and spleen meridians, dispersing wind and transforming phlegm. Initially use Bai Jie San combined with Wu He Tang, boiled with ginger and distilled lotus seed; then add Burdock Soup together with Dang Gui San, adding raw Rehmannia and brewing with ginger for consumption.[21p]

    　　　　　咽喉

    　　《心鉴》云：咽喉为一身之总要，与胃气相接，呼吸之所从出。若胸膈之间，蕴积热毒，致生风痰，壅滞不散，发而为咽喉之病，喉内生疮，或状如肉腐，为肿为痛，窒塞不通，吐咽不下，甚则生出重舌。治之尤重先去风痰，以通咽膈，然后解其热毒，迟则有不救之患。又有热毒冲于上腭而生疮，谓之悬痈及腑寒，亦能令人咽闭，吞吐不利。临病详审治之！　　咽喉之疾，本伤热毒上攻也。四时受热，藏心腑之间，一日所触上攻咽喉，所谓肾伤寒也。然其证有单肉蛾、双肉蛾，有重舌、木舌、痄腮，有悬瘫肿胀，有里外皆肿，甚者上攻头面皆肿。大法先洗去口中舌上白胎，其次扫去风涎。如是单双肉蛾，可针则针；有不可针者，则用熏掺药退后，方依次用服药。如是木舌，服药之外，仍用掺药。痄腮则用涂药，轻者但服药而自退，不须用针及药点，其疮自消也。[22p]

    Throat

    The "Heart Mirror" states: The throat is the crucial part of the body, connected with the stomach qi, and the place from which breathing emerges. If in the chest and diaphragm there accumulates heat and toxins, leading to the generation of wind-phlegm, which becomes stagnant and unresolved, it manifests as diseases of the throat—ulcers may form inside the throat, or appear as decayed flesh, resulting in swelling and pain, creating an obstruction that hinders swallowing, and in severe cases, a heavy tongue may develop. In treatment, it is essential to first eliminate wind-phlegm to clear the throat and diaphragm, and then resolve the heat and toxins; if treatment is delayed, serious consequences may ensue. Moreover, if heat toxins invade the soft palate causing ulcers, it is known as hanging sore or intestinal cold, which can also lead to throat closure and difficulty in swallowing. When faced with illness, treat it diligently!

    The diseases of the throat mainly stem from the attack of heat toxins. Throughout the seasons, these can harm the heart and viscera, and daily exposures can attack the throat, this is referred to as kidney cold injury. Symptoms include single or double flesh worms, heavy tongue, wooden tongue, mumps, and hanging swellings; severe cases may cause swelling of the head and face from the upward attack. The general principle is first to cleanse the white coating on the tongue, then to dispel wind saliva. For single or double flesh worms, if they are suitable for needling, then needle them; if they are unsuitable, use fumigating powders to retreat them, afterwards apply internal medications. For wooden tongue, aside from taking medicines, continue using medicinal powders. In cases of mumps, apply topical medications; mild cases may resolve with just oral medications, without the need for needling or medicinal points, allowing the ulcers to heal on their own.[22p]

    　　　　外科正宗 【明　陈实功】

    　　　　　鹅口疮

    　　鹅口疮皆心脾二经胎热上攻，致满口皆生白斑雪片，甚则咽间迭迭肿起，致难乳哺，多生啼叫。以青纱一条，裹着头上，蘸新汲水揩去白胎，以净为度，重手出血不妨，随以冰硼散搽之，内服凉膈之药。[23p]

    Throat Candidiasis

    Throat candidiasis is primarily caused by the excessive heat from the heart and spleen channels, which leads to the appearance of white patches resembling snowflakes throughout the mouth. In severe cases, there can be significant swelling in the throat, making breastfeeding difficult and resulting in frequent crying. Wrap a piece of blue gauze around the head and use fresh spring water to wipe away the white patches for purification. It is acceptable for the process to cause some bleeding; afterward, apply ice and borax powder, and administer cooling herbal medicine internally.[23p]

    　　　　　重舌

    　　小儿重舌，乃心火妄动发之。当以线针点刺患上，令出恶血，内服解毒泻心汤，外以冰硼散搽之。又有紫舌、木舌，亦由心火而发。用飞盐加冰片少许搽，出涎自愈。又有痰气结于舌上，成核作痛硬强者，用线针点破出血，用冰硼散搽之，服黄连泻心汤。
    　　　　　走马疳

    　　走马疳，言患迅速不可迟延故也。其患多由痧痘余毒所中，又有杂病热甚而成者。其患牙根作烂，随便黑腐作臭，甚者牙龈脱落，根柯黑朽，不数日间，以致穿腮破唇，诚为不治。初起宜用芦荟消疳饮，外用人中白散，或冰硼散二药搽之，取去黑腐肉，见红肉血流者为吉。如取时顽肉不脱，腐烂渐开，焮肿外散，臭味不止，更兼身热不退者，俱为不治。
    　　　　　牙疳五不治

    　　口臭涎秽者，一不治，黑腐不脱者，二不治；牙落无血者，三不治；穿腮破唇者，四不治；用药不效者，五不治。
    　　　　小儿卫生总微论方 【宋，撰人未详】[24p]

    Heavy Tongue

    A child's heavy tongue is caused by excessive heart fire. One should pierce the affected area with a fine needle to release the bad blood, and internally take a detoxifying Heart-Resolving Decoction. Externally, apply Ice Borax Powder. There are also conditions like purple tongue and wood tongue, which arise from heart fire. Apply a little flying salt mixed with a small amount of borneol to treat it, and it may heal by itself with saliva. If phlegm and qi are trapped on the tongue, forming painful and hard lumps, use a fine needle to pierce and let it bleed. Then apply Ice Borax Powder and take Huang Lian Heart-Resolving Decoction.

    Running Horse Sore

    The term "Running Horse Sore" indicates a rapid onset that cannot be delayed. It often arises from residual toxins of measles and smallpox, as well as from excessive heat of various diseases. The symptoms include rotten gums, black decay that emits a foul smell, and, in severe cases, loss of gums with roots turning black and decaying. Within a few days, this can lead to perforated cheeks and split lips, making it truly difficult to cure. At the onset, it is advisable to use Aloe Vera Decoction to dispel the sore, and externally apply Ren Zhong Bai Powder or Ice Borax Powder to remove black necrotic tissue, revealing red flesh and flowing blood, which is a good sign. If stubborn meat does not fall away, rotting continues to open, swelling spreads outward, and the foul odor persists along with persistent body heat, it is considered incurable.

    Five Incurable Tooth Sores

    1. Bad breath and filthy saliva: Incurable.
    2. Black necrotic tissue that does not come off: Incurable.
    3. Teeth falling out without blood: Incurable.
    4. Perforated cheeks and split lips: Incurable.
    5. No effectiveness from medication: Incurable.[24p]

    　　　　　唇口病论

    　　风毒湿热，随其虚处所著，搏于血气，则坐疮疡。若发于唇上生疮，乍瘥乍发，谓之紧唇，又曰沉唇。其发频者，唇常肿大粗厚，或上有疮不效，甚者以至唇腆。若发于唇里，连两颊生疮者，名曰口疮。若发于口吻两角生疮者，名曰燕口。俗云因乳食看视燕子，则生燕口疮也。
    　　　　　弄舌论

    　　小儿弄舌者，其证有二：一者心热。心系舌本，热则舌本干濇而紧，故时时吐弄舒缓之。二者脾热。脾络连舌，热则舌亦干濇而紧，故时时吐弄舒缓之。皆欲饮水。心热则发渴，脾热则津液耗，皆引饮。二证相似，宜加审别。心热者面赤，睡即口中气热，时时烦躁，喜就其冷，咬牙上窜，治宜退热。脾热者大便稠硬，赤黄色，面黄身亦微黄，治宜微导之，不可用冷药，又不可转下；若悞下之，则脾胃虚，津液耗，又加五心烦热，面黄肌瘦，变为疳也。若大病未已，用药后弄舌者，大凶也。以人参知母散、泻黄散治之。[25p]

    Discussion on Lip Diseases

    Wind, toxin, dampness, and heat attach themselves where there is deficiency. When they interact with the blood and qi, they cause sores and ulcers. If they appear on the lips as sores that intermittently heal and then reappear, it is called "tight lips" or "heavy lips." If they occur frequently, the lips become swollen and thick, sometimes even with lingering sores, leading to lip deformity. If they arise inside the lips, forming sores that connect to both cheeks, it is referred to as "oral sores." If they occur at the corners of the mouth, they are called "swallow's mouth." It is commonly said that this is due to dairy and food observing swallows, which causes swallow's mouth sores.

    Discussion on Tongue Manipulation

    When young children manipulate their tongues, there are two indications: one is heart heat. The heart is connected to the root of the tongue; when it is hot, the root becomes dry and tense, prompting the child to frequently stick out their tongue in a relaxed manner. The second is spleen heat. The spleen is connected to the tongue; when it is hot, the tongue also becomes dry and tense, leading to the same behavior. Both cases cause a desire for water. Heart heat results in thirst, while spleen heat causes depletion of fluids, which both provoke drinking. These two conditions are similar and should be examined carefully. A child with heart heat has a red face, experiences heat in the mouth while sleeping, is often restless, prefers coolness, and may grind their teeth. Treatment should focus on reducing heat. A child with spleen heat has hard, yellow stools, a yellowish face, and slight bodily jaundice; treatment should involve gentle guiding, avoiding cold medicines and excessive purging. If forcefully purged, it can lead to spleen and stomach deficiency, fluid depletion, and aggravate the child's restlessness and emaciation, ultimately resulting in malnutrition. If tongue manipulation occurs after a serious illness and medication, it is a very bad sign. Treatment with Ginseng Zhimu Powder and Xiahuang Powder is recommended.[25p]

    　　　　　舌病论

    　　小儿舌上偶生疮肿者，由风毒邪热搏于血气，随其虚处着而生病也。发于舌上紫肿者，名曰紫舌胀。若肿粗大，木闷而硬者，名曰木舌胀。若风湿相搏而生疮者，名曰舌疮。若风多而舌肿如吹胞者，名曰鼓舌。其紫舌木舌鼓舌肿甚者，则满口溢出，塞闭气门，皆能杀人。
    　　　　　咽喉病论

    　　小儿咽喉生病者，由风毒湿热搏于气血，随其经络虚处所著，则生其病。若发于咽喉者，或为喉痹，或为缠喉风，或为乳鹅；重者或为马喉痹，又或悬痈肿，或腮颔肿，或喉中生疮。
    　　　　　诸物梗喉论[26p]

    On Tongue Diseases

    When a child develops sores or swelling on the tongue, it results from the invasion of wind, toxins, and heat affecting the vital energy and blood. If the tongue presents with purple swelling, it is referred to as "purple tongue swelling." If the swelling is large and firm, it is called "hard tongue swelling." If sores appear due to the clash of wind and dampness, it is termed "tongue sores." If there is an abundance of wind and the tongue swells like a blowfish, it is known as "drum tongue." Severe cases of purple tongue, hard tongue, or drum tongue may lead to excessive salivation, blocking of the airway, and can be fatal.

    On Throat Diseases

    When a child suffers from throat diseases, it is caused by the interaction of wind, toxins, dampness, and heat affecting the vital energy and blood, targeting weak points along the meridians, leading to illness. If it occurs in the throat, it may manifest as throat obstruction, a type of throat wind, or "goose milk." In serious cases, it could lead to horse throat paralysis, or may present as abscesses or swelling in the jaw and throat, or sores within the throat.

First, puncture the swollen area to draw blood, rinse the mouth with salt water, and apply the medicine inside.

    Yi Nie Jin San: Treats children with thrush, mouth sores, heavy tongue, and wooden tongue. Ingredients: Xiong Huang 3 qian; Borax 1 qian; Gan Cao 0.5 qian; a little piece of Nao. Crush these into a fine powder, apply dry to the affected area, or mix with honey for application.

    Ge's Prescription: Treats children with thrush. Ingredients: Huang Dan—roasted and finely powdered with black water; apply to the tongue to heal, and continue taking the disinfecting drink.

    Xi Jiao Disinfecting Drink: Treats infants with wind toxin, red-purple sore lumps, strong fever, agitation, unrest during sleep, chest fullness, swollen and painful throat, blood improperly flowing from the nine orifices, and rash throughout the body. Ingredients: Stir-fried Niu PZ, 1.5 liang; Jing Jie Sui 5 qian; Sheng Gan Cao and Fang Feng, each 2.5 qian; Xi Jiao 1.5 qian. Grind into a powder, and decoct with water, to be taken without restriction on time.

    Xie Huang San: Treats children with excess heat in the stomach meridian, causing throat obstruction, grinding teeth, heart and spleen heat accumulation leading to tongue sticking out. Ingredients: Huo Xiang Ye 7 qian; Shan Zhi 1 liang; Shi Gao and Gan Cao each 5 qian; Fang Feng 4 liang. Grind these into a powder, and gently stir-fry with honey wine until fragrant. For each dose, take 2 qian, decocked in water.[30p]

    　　胡黄连丸　治小儿五心烦热，面黄弄舌。　　川黄连　胡黄连各半两　朱砂一分，另研　将二连为细末，入朱砂末，填入猪胆内，用淡水煮，以杖安铫子上，用绵钓之，勿着底，候一炊久取出，研入芦荟、麝香各一分，饭和丸如麻子大，每服五七丸至一二十丸。食后米饮下。一作食前，治疳证有热者。一方加虾(虫麻)半两，不烧。
    　　青液散　治婴孩鹅口，重舌，口疮。　　青黛一钱　(石卜)硝一钱　冰片少许　　右为细末，蜜调，以鹅翎少许敷上。一方去(石卜)硝。
    　　一字散
    　　朱砂　冰片各少许　蜜调，鹅翎刷口内，咽下无妨。
    　　芎黄散　治齿生迟，或嚼物少力，此方主之。　　川芎五钱　山药　当归酒炒　白芍药炒　甘草灸，各二钱半　　右为细末，用白汤调化，食后服；或将干药末掺齿断。一方加生地半两，去芍药。[31p]

    Hu Huanglian Pill: Treats children's five hearts vexation and heat, yellowish face, and playing with the tongue.

    Ingredients: Equal parts of Chuan Huanglian and Hu Huanglian (each half a tael), one fen of cinnabar, to be ground separately. Combine the two Huanglians into a fine powder, then mix in the cinnabar powder, and fill into a pig's gallbladder. Boil in plain water, using a stick to stabilize a ladle above, ensuring it does not touch the bottom. Once cooked for a sufficient duration, take out and grind together with one fen each of aloe and musk. Form into pills the size of sesame seeds, taking five to seven pills up to twenty pills after meals. Some suggest taking them before meals, especially to treat cases of "gan" (malnutrition) with heat. Another method adds half a tael of shrimp (or silkworm).

    Qingye Powder: Treats infants with thrush, heavy tongue, and mouth ulcers.

    Ingredients: One qian of indigo, one qian of (litharge) nitrate, a pinch of ice flakes. Grind into a fine powder and mix with honey. Use a small goose feather to apply.

    Yi Zi Powder:

    Ingredients: A small amount each of cinnabar and ice flakes mixed with honey, applied to the inside of the mouth with a goose feather, swallowing is not a problem.

    Xiong Huang Powder: Treats delayed tooth eruption or weak chewing ability.

    Ingredients: Five qian of Chuan Xiong, two and a half qian each of yam, fried Angelica, fried white peony, and moxa. Grind into a fine powder and mix with white broth for consumption after meals; an alternative is to sprinkle the dry powder on broken teeth. Another method adds half a tael of fresh Rehmannia and omits the peony.[31p]

    　　金星丸　治小儿风热壅盛，喉中痰鸣，嗽喘气粗，面颊红，腮赤肿痛，咽喉壅塞，目闭不开，多眠发热，狂言烦躁多渴则生惊风，大便不通，小便如血，诸般热壅，疮痍烦躁，并宜服之。　　真郁金　雄黄飞，各二钱半　腻粉煅，半钱　巴豆七粒，去油　　右为末，调匀，酢糊为丸麻子大，薄荷汤下。
    　　连翘漏芦汤　治小儿痈疮，丹毒，疮疖，咽喉肿痛，腮肿。　　漏芦　麻黄去根节　连翘　升麻　黄芩　白蔹各一钱　甘草　枳壳各半钱　　右为粗末，每服一钱，以水一小盏，煎至五分去滓，量儿大小，不拘时温服。热甚加大黄、(石卜)硝。
    　　连翘汤　治疮疹壮热，小便不通，诸般疮疖，丹毒，脐风。　　连翘　瞿麦　荆芥　木通　当归　防风　赤芍药　柴胡　滑石　蝉蜕　甘草炙各一钱　山栀　黄芩各五分　　右銼细，每服二钱，加紫草，煎温服。热甚加大黄，更详证加减。[32p]

    Jinxing Pill: Treats excessive wind-heat in children, causing phlegm sounds in the throat, cough, wheezing, flushed cheeks, swollen and painful jaws, throat obstruction, inability to open eyes, excessive sleepiness accompanied by fever, wild talk, restlessness, and thirst that can lead to convulsions. Also for constipation and blood-like urine, various forms of heat obstruction and irritability from sores.

    Ingredients: True Eucommia, Realgar, each 2.5 qian; Niti powder, 0.5 qian; 7 seeds of Euphorbia, with oil removed. Grind into a fine powder, mix thoroughly, and form into pills the size of hemp seeds, taken with mint soup.

    Lianqiao and Luoluo Decoction: Treats children's carbuncles, scarlet fever, skin sores, throat pain, and swollen jaws.

    Ingredients: Luoluo (with roots removed), Mahuang; Lianqiao; Shengma; Huangqin; Bailian, each 1 qian; Licorice and Zhike, each 0.5 qian. Prepare a coarse powder. For each dose, take 1 qian with a small cup of water, decoct until reduced to 5 parts, and strain. Adjust quantity based on the child's size, and take warm as needed. If heat is severe, add Dahuang and (Shibai) Salts.

    Lianqiao Decoction: Treats rashes with strong heat, difficulty urinating, various sores and carbuncles, scarlet fever, and umbilical wind.

    Ingredients: Lianqiao; Qumai; Jingjie; Mutong; Danggui; Fangfeng; Chishaoyao; Chaihu; Huashi; Chentui; Licorice (roasted), each 1 qian; Shanzhi; Huangqin, each 0.5 qian.

    Prepare finely; for each dose, take 2 qian, add Zicao, and decoct for warm consumption. If heat is severe, add Dahuang; further adjust based on detailed symptoms.[32p]

    　　清凉饮子　治小儿百病，变蒸客忤，惊癎壮热，痰涎壅盛，烦闷颊赤，口干烦渴，项颈结热，头面疮疖，肚中热痛。　　大黄　连翘　芍药　羌活　当归　防风　甘草　山栀仁各等分　　右銼散，每服二钱，水半盏，煎三分，去滓，不拘时服。

    Cooling Drink treats all diseases of children: it alleviates steam and heat, surprises, convulsions, excessive phlegm, irritability, red cheeks, dry mouth and thirst, neck heat and stiffness, sores on the head and face, and abdominal heat and pain.
    Ingredients:

    • Dahuang (Rhubarb)
    • Lianqiao (Forsythia)
    • Shaoyao (Peony)
    • Qianghuo (Notopterygium)
    • Danggui (Angelica)
    • Fangfeng (Siler)
    • Gancao (Licorice)
    • Shanzhizi (Gardenia fruit), all in equal parts.

    Grind the above into a fine powder. For each dose, take two qian (a unit of weight), mix with half a bowl of water, simmer for three minutes, strain, and take at any time.

    Yihuang Powder treats children's vomiting and diarrhea, as well as a weak spleen that cannot digest food, leading to fatigue and a tendency to have loose stools at night; also for deficiency, night sweats, and fullness in the cheeks.
    Ingredients:

    • Chenpi (Dried tangerine peel, white part removed) - 1 liang
    • Dingxiang (Clove) - 2 qian
    • Hezi (Chebula fruit, roasted and pit removed) - 5 qian
    • Qingpi (Green tangerine peel, the hard part removed) - 5 qian
    • Gancao (Licorice) - 5 qian.

    Grind the above into powder. For each dose, take two qian, simmer with water for three minutes, and take before meals. Alternatively, substitute Dingxiang with Muxiang (Agarwood).

    Wenpi Dan (Warm Spleen Pill) for fullness in the cheeks.
    Ingredients:

    • Banxia (Pinellia) - 1 liang
    • Dingxiang (Clove) - 1 liang
    • Muxiang (Agarwood) - 1 liang
    • Ganjiang (Dried ginger) - 0.5 liang
    • Baizhu (Atractylodes) - 0.5 liang
    • Qingpi (Green tangerine peel) - 0.5 liang
    • Chenpi (Dried tangerine peel) - 0.5 liang.

    Grind into powder, form into pills the size of a grain of millet. For a one-year-old, take ten pills; for a two-year-old, twenty pills, adjusting as necessary, taken with rice soup.

    Bingbeng Powder treats soreness and swelling in the throat and teeth, prolonged cough with phlegm and fire, and hoarseness with pain.
    Ingredients:

    • Bingpian (Borneol) - 0.5 qian
    • Feiguo (Cinnabar) - 0.6 qian (refined to Yanmingsuan)
    • Borax - 0.5 qian.

    Grind into very fine powder and apply to the affected area. For severe cases, apply five to six times a day for best results.[33p]

    Formula for Treating Mouth Sores in Children

    For treating children's mouth sores and tight lips:

    • Peppermint
    • Coptis
      Mix them equally into a powder, then add a small amount of indigo and apply.

    Lead Frost Powder
    Used for the same condition as above:

    • Lead frost
    • Mung bean flour (each half a liang)
      Grind them together and mix with the juice of rapeseed for application.

    Sweet Dew Drink
    For treating excess heat in a child's stomach, swollen and decayed gums, occasional purulent and bloody discharges, mouth ulcers, and sore throat:

    • Stir-fried bitter orange peel
    • Dendrobium
    • Loquat leaves (hair removed)
    • Cooked rehmannia
    • Fresh baicalin
    • Mountain gentian
    • Ophiopogon (heart removed)
    • Fresh rehmannia
    • Asparagus (heart removed)
      Each one qian
    • Licorice (roasted), five fen

    Prepare one dose using two zhong of water, decoct until reduced to seven parts, and administer after meals. In the "Ben Shi Fang," without ophiopogon or gentian, add mountain bean root and rhinoceros horn shavings for significant efficacy.

    Holy Powder
    For treating children's mouth sores that prevent them from sucking:

    • One seed of Jiangzi (Chinese yew)
    • Small amounts of vermilion and yellow lead oxide

    Remove the skin from the Jiangzi and grind it into a paste without removing the oil. Mix in the other two ingredients, apply on paper or silk, part the child's fontanelle, and place this on top. If sores form at the edges, wash off the medicine with warm water to avoid wounds; rinse with calamus water for miraculous effects. There is a recipe without vermilion.[34p]

    Di Gu Pi Wan 【"Rumen"】
    For treating pediatric lung heat, characterized by a mouth like glue, dry tongue, thirst, and frequent urination.
    Ingredients: equal parts of Di Gu Pi, Huang Qi, Sang Bai Pi, Shan Zhi, and Ma Dou Ling.
    Grind them into a fine powder, mix with Glycyrrhiza paste to form pills the size of Job's tears. Allow each pill to dissolve in the mouth after meals.

    Bing Liang Wan 【"Liang Fang"】
    For treating oral sores in children.
    Ingredients: a small amount of Dragon Brain, equal parts of Huang Bo, Borax, and Mint leaves.
    Grind them to a fine powder, mix well, and form pills the size of longan. Take one pill each time, allowing saliva to wash down. For severe sores, increase the amount of Dragon Brain.

    Jia Jian Xie Bai San 【"Zhi Zhi Fang"】
    For treating guest heat in the stomach, characterized by bad breath and sores.
    Ingredients: 1 qian each of Sang Bai Pi, Di Gu Pi, roasted Licorice, Zhi Mu, and Huang Qin; 7 fen each of Wu Wei Zi, Mai Men Dong, and Jie Geng.
    Chew the ingredients, boil in water, strain, and take warm away from meals. Avoid spicy and hot foods.

    Sheng Xiang Gao 【"Lei Yao"】
    Ingredients: 0.5 qian of Huang Bo and 2 qian of Luo Qing.
    Grind finely, and apply one character or half a qian to the affected area.

    Bing Lang San 【"Da Quan"】
    For treating various oral sores.
    Ingredients: equal parts of Bing Lang, Copper Green, and Fritillaria.[35p]

    Warm Stomach Powder
    Treated for excessive cold phlegm in the spleen, causing stagnation in the jaw.

    • Clove: 1 tael
    • Ginseng: ½ tael
    • Pinellia: ½ tael
    • Nutmeg: ½ tael
    • Atractylodes: ½ tael
    • Dried ginger: ½ tael
    • Licorice: ½ tael

    Grind the above into a powder. Take 1 qian with ginger water prepared by boiling. Xue Ji said: According to this formula, it treats weakness and cold of the spleen and stomach, ceaseless phlegm flow, or good for vomiting and abdominal pain. After warming the spleen qi slightly, take Wuwei Yigong powder.

    Musk Powder from Zhuang Family
    Used for children with foul, rotten odors from the mouth and gums.

    • Musk: 1 qian
    • Realgar: 1 qian
    • Aloe: 1 qian
    • Dragon bone: 1 qian
    • Miltong: 2 qian
    • Stone gall: ½ tael
    • Live, dried toad: ½ tael

    Burn them in a bottle to preserve their properties. Grind them together until very fine. Take a cotton pad wrapped around a stick, lightly wash it with salted alum water, then apply the medicine.

    Kale Root Powder
    Used for children with tightly closed lips.

    • Kale root: 1 tael (ashes)
    • Black snake ash: ½ tael
    • Coptis: powdered fine, ½ tael
    • Soft-shelled turtle shell ash: ½ tael

    Take ½ qian of the mixture, mix with a little pig fat, and apply to the lips occasionally.

    Ash Powder
    Used for children with sores around the mouth that do not soften after a long time.

    • Burnt hair: equal parts
    • Cotton ash: equal parts
    • Coptis (without soil): equal parts
    • Dried ginger: equal parts

    Grind to a powder. Apply a small amount up to three times, and it will heal.[36p]

    Seven-Flavored Bai Zhu Powder
    Treats children who have sticking out or playing with their tongues due to dietary harm and spleen-stomach weakness, leading to "horse teeth."
    Ingredients: Ginseng, white poria, Bai Zhu (Atractylodes), Huo Xiang leaves, Mu Xiang, licorice, dry kudzu.
    Prepare by boiling with water, adjusting the dosage according to the child's size.

    Wubozhi Powder (from "Zheng Zhi Zhun Sheng")
    Treats loosening teeth or injuries from foreign objects when other medicines are ineffective and teeth are about to fall out.
    Ingredients: Sichuan Wubozhi, dried earth dragon (lightly roasted), both in equal amounts.
    Grind into a fine powder. First rub the tooth roots with fresh ginger, then apply the powdered medicine. Avoid biting hard objects for five days. If a tooth is just about to fall out, hot compress can be applied to the tooth socket and medicine placed on the tooth to secure it as before.

    Dao Chi Powder (from "Xue's Medical Cases")
    Treats children with weak heat and teeth grinding, and heat in the small intestine channel affecting the throat.
    Ingredients: Fresh Rehmannia, Muntiacum, licorice in equal parts.
    Grind into a powder. Each dose is one qian, boiled in light bamboo leaf water.

    Chai Hu Qing Gan Powder
    Treats children with excess heat in the liver channel causing tooth grinding and wind-heat leading to throat obstruction.
    Ingredients: Chai Hu, roasted Huang Qin, ginseng, Sichuan Chuanxiong, roasted gardenia, each one qian; Lian Qiao, licorice, and Jie Geng, each 5 fen.
    Prepare by boiling with water and consume.

    Xie Bai Powder
    Treats children with excess heat in the lung channel causing tooth grinding, leading to throat obstruction.
    Ingredients: Roasted white mulberry bark, di gu pi (dried root of Lycium), roasted licorice, all in equal parts.
    Grind into a powder, boiling with one hundred grains of polished rice in water.[37p]

    　　桃红散 【《保幼大全》】 　治小儿牙痈，肿烂脓血。　　朱砂一钱，研水飞　菉豆粉一两　硼砂半钱　片脑　麝香各一字　　右为末，每用一字敷患处，或揩贴之。
    　　立效饮 【《证治准绳》，下同】 　治小儿牙根舌上发疮作痛，致言语饮食不便。　　净黄连一两　　北细辛去叶，二钱半　元明粉二钱　　右细銼，或晒或焙为末，仍同元明粉乳钵内杵匀，每用一字，干点患处，或以一钱新汲井水调涂疮上。儿小者畏苦不肯点咽，用蜜水调敷患处，令其自化。咽痛茶清调下。[38p]

    Yi Gong San Qian Shi: For treating children with a weak stomach due to heat and teeth grinding. Ingredients include equal parts of ginseng, white atractylodes, poria, stir-fried licorice, and aged tangerine peel. Grind to a fine powder and decoct in water for consumption.

    Jia Wei Xiao Yao San Xue Shi: For treating children who grind their teeth at night due to wind-heat interaction leading to throat obstruction. Ingredients include 1 qian of angelica, stir-fried licorice, and wine-fried peony root; 1 qian respectively of poria, stir-fried white atractylodes, and bupleurum; and 7 fen each of stir-fried gardenia and peony bark. Decoct in water for consumption.

    Tao Hong San (from "Bao You Da Quan"): For treating children's dental abscesses with swelling, pus, and blood. Ingredients include 1 qian of cinnabar, finely ground and suspended in water; 1 liang of mung bean powder; ½ qian of borax; and 1 character each of powdered lead and musk. Grind to a fine powder and apply 1 character to the affected area, or use as a poultice.

    Li Xiao Yin (from "Zheng Zhi Zhun Sheng", same below): For treating painful sores at the roots of teeth or on the tongue, causing difficulties in speaking and eating. Ingredients include 1 liang of clean huanglian, 2.5 qian of north asarum leaves removed, and 2 qian of yuanming powder. Finely grind or sun-dry and toast, then mix thoroughly in a mortar. Use 1 character to dry the affected area or mix 1 qian of freshly drawn well water to apply to the sores. For children who fear bitterness and refuse to swallow, use honey water as a dressing so it can resolve naturally. A tea can also be prepared to treat throat pain.[38p]

    　　黄金散　解口内舌上疮毒，及治痘疮后目生翳膜。　　黄蘗用生蜜润透，烈日晒干，再涂蜜晒，凡十数次　粉草各一两　　右銼研为细末。治口疮用药末干点患处；或用麦门冬熟水调点舌上，令其自化。若痘疮后目生翳膜，汤泡澄清，无时频洗，仍投糖煎散、柿煎散二药。
    　　天竺黄散　治上焦风热，口鼻生疮，两目赤肿，咽膈不利，痰涎壅滞，气不通畅，惊搐烦闷，神思昏迷。　　天竺黄　郁金无，山栀仁代　茯神去皮根　甘草各半两　硼砂　牙硝　白芷　川芎　僵蚕　枳壳麸炒微黄，各二钱半　朱砂飞，二钱　麝香一字　蝉壳十五枚，洗去泥土嘴足　　右除硼砂、牙硝、朱砂、麝香四味，乳钵细杵，余九味焙干为末，同入乳钵内，再杵匀，每服半钱或一钱，温薄荷汤无时调服，或麦门冬汤。[39p]

    Golden Powder
    For treating sores and toxins on the tongue, and for clearing membrane obstruction after smallpox.
    Take Huangbai mixed with raw honey to thoroughly soak, dry in the hot sun, then reapply honey and dry again, for about ten times. Powder each of the herbs, one liang each.
    For mouth sores, apply the dry powdered medicine directly to the affected area; or mix with cooked Mai Men Dong water and apply to the tongue to let it self-dissolve. If a membrane appears in the eyes post-smallpox, soak and rinse with clear broth frequently, and also use sugar powder and persimmon powder.

    Ten Bamboo Yellow Powder
    For treating wind-heat in the upper body, sores in the mouth and nose, red and swollen eyes, obstructed throat, phlegm and saliva stagnation, unimpeded qi, and symptoms of shock, restlessness, and clouded consciousness.
    Ingredients: Tian Zhu Huang, Yu Jin (without), substitute with Shan Zhi Ren; Fu Shen (peeled, root), Gan Cao (each half a liang), Borax, Yashao, Bai Zhi, Chuan Xiong, Jiang Can, Zhi Ke (lightly fried until yellow), each two qian and five fen; Zhu Sha (two qian, powdered), a single word of Shexiang, and fifteen pieces of Chan Ke (washed of dirt).
    Remove Borax, Yashao, Zhu Sha, and Shexiang, and finely pound the remaining nine ingredients into a powder, mix them well in a mortar. Each dose is half a qian or one qian, mixed with warm mint tea at any time, or Mai Men Dong soup.[39p]

    　　香附散张涣方　治齿不生。
    　　香附拣净刮去皮　沉香各一两　雄鼠粪烧灰　干蟾烧灰　槟榔各半两　　右件捣罗为细末，用羊髓四两煮烂，和成膏，如黍米大，每服十粒，麝香汤下。量儿大小加减。
    　　清胃散薛氏　治胃火牙痛，或连头面，膏粱积热，致生喉痹。　　升麻五分　生地黄　牡丹皮　川黄连炒　当归各三分　　右水煎服。加柴胡、山栀，即加味清胃散。薛己曰：愚按前方治脾胃实火作渴，口舌生疮，或唇口肿痛，齿龈溃烂，焮连头面，或恶寒发热，或重舌马牙，吐舌流涎等证，子母并宜服之。若因脾胃气虚，寒凉克伐，或虚热上行，口舌生疮，弄舌发热，饮食少思；或呕吐困睡，大便不实，流涎龈烂者，用五味异功散。[40p]

    Xiangfu Powder by Zhang Huan
    For the treatment of non-erupting teeth.
    Xiangfu, cleaned and peeled; each of sandalwood one tael; male rat droppings, burned to ash; dried toad, burned to ash; betel nut, each half a tael. Combine the above ingredients into a fine powder, using four taels of sheep marrow, cooked until soft, to form a paste the size of millet. Take ten pellets each time, swallowed with musk-infused decoction. Adjust dosage according to the child's size.

    Clear Stomach Powder by Xue Family
    For treating stomach fire toothache, which may extend to the head and face, heat accumulated from rich foods leading to throat paralysis.
    Five fen of licorice; three fen each of raw rehmannia root, peony root, and stir-fried huanglian; three fen of angelica.
    Decoct the ingredients in water for consumption. If adding Chaihu and mountain gardenia, it is an enhanced version of Clear Stomach Powder. Xue Ji notes: My humble opinion is that the previous formula treats excessive heat from the spleen and stomach causing thirst, ulcers on the tongue and mouth, or swollen, painful lips, with gums ulcerated, affecting the head and face; also for symptoms of chills and fever, or the tongue appearing thick, drooling, etc. Both mothers and children should take it. However, if due to spleen and stomach qi deficiency, cold dampness invading, or deficiency heat rising, leading to tongue ulcers, heat in the tongue, diminished appetite, or symptoms like vomiting, drowsiness, loose stools, and ulcerated gums, Wu Wei Di Huang San should be used.[40p]

    　　藁本散 【《证治准绳》，下同】 　治卒齿痛，及小儿风蚛牙痛。　　槁本　白附子　川芎　莽草各半两，并末，次用　青黛　芦荟　麝香各一钱，研细　　右件都再研匀，每用一字，涂揩患处。

    Gao Ben San
    For treating tooth pain in adults and teething pain in children.
    Take equal parts of Gao Ben, Bai Fu Zi, Chuan Xiong, and Mang Cao, each half a tael, and grind them into a fine powder. Next, add one qian each of Qing Dai, Lu Hui, and She Xiang, and grind finely. Mix everything, and apply a small amount to the affected area.

    Xiong Huang Wan
    For treating black cavities and painful breath in children.
    Take two qian of Xiong Huang and half a qian of She Xiang. Grind them into a fine powder, mix with soft rice to form a paste, and place it inside the tooth.

    Tooth Gums Swelling Pain Recipe
    Take three taels each of Sheng Di Huang and Du Huo, cut them and soak in wine overnight.

    Another Recipe
    For swollen tooth roots.
    Take a handful of pine needles, one he of salt, and three sheng of good wine. Boil these together to obtain one sheng, and use it as a rinse.

    Another Recipe
    For swollen and painful tooth roots, causing distress and discomfort.
    Take four taels of Du Huo and three sheng of wine. Soak in a container and warm over a fire, bringing it to a gentle boil until reduced by half. Strain and rinse with the hot liquid, not exceeding four or five doses.

    Another Recipe
    For painful tooth gums.[41p]

    One hundred almonds, removing the skin, tips, and double kernels; a pinch of salt. The two ingredients above, boil with one liter of water until the foam rises. Hold in the mouth, taste until it's gone, then spit it out and continue holding, but do not do this more than three times.

    The "Holy Benefit Shrimp (Insect Hemp) Powder" treats children's toothaches, wind cavities, and slight swelling of the jaw. One dried shrimp (Insect Hemp); one slice of indigo; one slice of tangerine peel; one slice of fine xixin; one slice of white chicken dung; each of these is one part; a small amount of musk, finely ground; and half a slice of dried ginger, prepared and shredded. These ingredients should be ground finely and sifted to make a powder, then wrap a small amount in thin cotton and place it into the cavity daily, changing it.

    Another formula: one tael of white atractylodes, one tael of dried roots, one tael of fine xixin, one tael of chuanxiong, and one tael of dandelion. Grind these ingredients to a fine powder, then wrap a small amount in thin cotton and place it on the cavity.

    Another formula for treating children's wind cavities and painful tooth decay: one dried shrimp (Insect Hemp) burned to ash; one slice of indigo; half a slice of aloe. Grind these together finely, then boil with fresh rehmannia to create a paste, and apply it to the teeth.

    Another formula for treating children's painful wind cavities and tooth decay causing black rotting: finely ground indigo; burned white chicken dung ash; dried roots; north fine xixin; and finely ground realgar, each one slice; a small amount of musk, finely ground. Grind these ingredients together finely, and take a small amount to apply to the teeth.[42p]

    Gathering Treasure Yellow Dragon Powder (from "Essentials")
    For treating tooth decay and sores on the gums, when there are cavities that do not fit. The true dragon essence is found in the deep yellow or light yellow of dragon bone, when a tight scoop touches the tongue, it comprises: white alum, snail shell, southern powder, cow bile, each one qian. Grind these five ingredients into a powder, use a small amount each time, and apply it inside the cavity, using it regularly.

    Coptis and Gypsum Decoction (from "Miscellaneous Writings of Ming Physicians")
    For treating swollen gums in children, salivation, and swelling in the jaw, primarily for heat in the Yangming. Ingredients: seven fen of the following: schizonepeta, ligusticum chuanxiong, white peony root, and fried pinellia; five fen of the following: dioscorea, raw licorice, ledum, and fried coptis; one qian of the following: gypsum and white atractylodes; three fen of white angelica. Boil the above with water and take two qian each time. If possible, rinse with the medicine, then spit it out. Do not use white atractylodes or fried pinellia for rinsing.[43p]

    Four Gentlemen Decoction: Treats children with excessive thirst due to deficiency heat in the stomach. Ingredients: Ginseng, Atractylodes, Poria, and Honey-fried Licorice, each five fen. Prepare by decocting in water and take.

    Ginseng Stomach Calming Powder: Treats children's stomach deficiency with wind-heat, drooling at the mouth, or swelling in the cheeks, with tongue movement. Ingredients: Astragalus (2 qian), Ginseng (1 qian), dried tangerine peel without white, raw licorice, honey-fried licorice (each five fen), white peony (seven fen), white poria (four fen), and yellow bile (two fen). Grind into coarse powder, take 2-3 qian each time, decoct in water until boiling five times, strain, and take warm.

    Ginseng and Anemarrhena Powder: Treats lingering severe illness, with tongue movements after medication. Ingredients: Anemarrhena (1 liang), blue leaf (0.5 liang), Ginseng without the husk (0.5 liang), hop vine, Chuanxiong, kudzu root, and yellow gentian (each one fen). Grind into fine powder, take one qian each time, add eight portions of water and three drops of bamboo juice, decoct until it reduces to five portions, strain, and take warm at any time.

    Nitre Yellow Powder: Treats wind-heat attacking upwards, causing stiffness and swelling of the tongue. Ingredients: Sublimed ammonium nitrate and true pollen, each half a liang. Prepare by drying the pollen and grinding it finely, using the ammonium nitrate in a mortar, mix well, and apply to the tongue above and below.[45p]

    　　圣济当归散　治小儿脾肝心经为湿热风寒所中，致重舌木舌，或舌卷缩舒长，或肿满。　　当归去芦　白芍药　人参　甘草炙　桔梗　陈皮各一钱　　右(口父)咀，煎五分，时时少服。

    　　牛黄散　治脾脏积热，令舌络微紧，时时弄舌。　　牛黄研　朱砂研飞　麝香　天竺黄并细研　蝎梢　钓藤俱研末，各一分　　右件一处研匀，每服一字，新汲水调下。[46p]

    Green Robe Powder treats heavy tongue and sores inside and outside the mouth, as well as throat blockage. Ingredients include: five qian each of mint leaves and schizonepeta flower, two and a half qian each of indigo, alum, and borax, and three qian each of the Hundred Medicinal Decoction and licorice. Grind and roast these into a powder, except for the alum and borax, which should be finely ground in a mortar. Mix with the other ingredients until uniform, using a dose of up to half a qian applied directly to the tongue to let it dissolve; alternatively, you can mix it with freshly drawn water and honey and apply to the tongue as well.

    Sheng Ji Dang Gui Powder treats children's spleen, liver, and heart ailments caused by damp-heat and wind-cold, resulting in heavy tongue or curling and swelling of the tongue. Ingredients consist of one qian each of angelica (with the root stripped), white peony, ginseng, roasted licorice, platycodon root, and dried tangerine peel. Grind these, decoct for five minutes, and take small amounts from time to time.

    Qiang Huo Powder treats heavy tongue, curled tongue, and sores on the tongue. The formulation includes: one liang each of ginseng, qian huo, red poria, bupleurum, fang feng, chuanxiong, du huo, platycodon, bitter orange peel, and苍术, and licorice. Grind these, take two qian with one cup of water, two slices of ginger, and three leaves of mint, decoct for seven minutes, and take at any time.

    Niu Huang Powder treats accumulated heat in the spleen, leading to slight tension in the tongue's connections, causing tongue manipulation. The ingredients include: a fen each of niu huang (bezoar), vermilion, musk, and tian zhu huang (garnet), finely ground, as well as scorpion tail and fishing vine ground into powder. Mix these thoroughly, and take a dose with freshly drawn water to consume.[46p]

    　　天竺黄散　治小儿上焦极热，致生重舌、木舌、鹅口、重腭，并舌口上生疮。　　天竺黄研　郁金　山栀　白僵蚕炒去丝嘴　蝉壳去土　甘草各等分　　右为末，一岁半钱，熟水、薄荷汤皆可服，不拘时。
    　　朱砂膏　治同上。
    　　朱砂飞五钱　牙硝　硼砂　元明粉各二钱半　麝香一字　金箔　银箔各十五片　白附子　枳壳麸炒微黄，各三钱　川芎　粉草各四钱　人参去芦　黄苓　薄荷叶各二钱　　右銼为末，掺口内。

    　　玉露饮　治小儿木舌肿硬，不能乳食。　　寒水石中有细纹，手可碎者　石膏各一两　甘草晒干，天阴火焙，三钱　　右为细末，每服半钱至一钱，温汤无时调服。
    　　百解散　治小儿木舌。
    　　干葛　升麻　赤芍　黄芩　麻黄制　薄桂　甘草各等分　　右碎，水煎，无时温服。风热甚，加薄荷同煎。[47p]

    Tianzhu Huang San: Treats extreme heat in the upper burner for children, leading to symptoms such as heavy tongue, wood tongue, thrush, and ulcers on the tongue and mouth.

    Ingredients: Tianzhu Huang, ground; Yujin; Shan Zhi Zi; Bai Jiang Can, stir-fried and silk removed; Chan Ke, dirt removed; Gan Cao, all in equal parts.

    Grind into a powder; for children aged one year and a half, it can be taken with cooked water or mint soup at any time.

    Zhusha Gao: Treats the same condition.

    Ingredients: Zhusha (five qian); Yashao; Bōngshā; Yuanming Fen, each two and a half qian; Musk, one character; Gold leaf; Silver leaf, fifteen pieces each; Bai Fu Zi; Zhi Ke, stir-fried until slightly yellow, three qian each; Chuan Xiong; Fen Cao, each four qian; Ren Shen, remove the reeds; Huang Ling; Bo He, two qian each.

    Grind into a powder and apply inside the mouth.

    Yulu Drink: Treats children with swollen hard wood tongues that cannot suckle or eat.

    Ingredients: Han Shui Shi with fine lines, that can be crushed by hand; G plaster, each one liang; Gan Cao, sun-dried and baked on a cloudy day, three qian.

    Grind into a fine powder; take half a qian to one qian with warm soup at any time.

    Bai Jie San: Treats wood tongue in children.

    Ingredients: Gan Ge; Sheng Ma; Chi Shao; Huang Qin; Ma Huang, processed; Bo Gui; Gan Cao, all in equal parts.

    Crush and decoct in water, take warm at any time. If wind-heat is severe, add Bo He to decoct together.[47p]

    　　五和汤　治木舌。
    　　当归酒洗　赤茯苓去皮，各半两　炙草　大黄　枳壳水浸润去穰銼片，麦麸炒微黄，各七钱半　　右水煎，无时温服。
