    Wuhuo Decoction treats wooden tongue.
    Wash angelica wine, peel red poria, both half a tael; fried licorice, rhubarb; bitter orange, soaked in water and filtered into thin slices; wheat bran, lightly fried to a pale yellow, each seven and a half qian. Boil with water, take warm at any time.

    Jin Zhu Drink treats excessive heat from fright, exogenous febrile diseases, internal heat in the upper jiao, heavy tongue, mouth and nose sores, and red eyes, among other symptoms.
    Chuan yujin, chopped and boiled, dried well; bamboosa; fried licorice; prepared natron, each half a tael; powdered cinnabar, one fen finely ground; fourteen cicada shells; a little musk. Prepare into a powder, take half a qian to one qian, mixed with honeyed water.

    (Shibu) nitre powder treats children's wooden tongue.
    Nitre, one tael; true purple snow, five qian; salt, two and a half qian. Prepare into a fine powder, take five fen, add two taels of bamboo juice, and adjust with white soup to apply to the tongue, swallowing saliva is fine.

    Wuyufang by Zhang Huan treats children's heavy tongue.
    Fishbone, one tael; beetle ash; fried catkin pollen, each five qian; dry white alum, two and a half qian. Prepare into a very fine powder, mix with egg yolk to apply under the tongue, swallowing saliva is fine.

    Angelica and Forsythia Decoction treats children's heart and spleen heat leading to heavy tongue.
    Angelica tails; forsythia; Chuan white atractylodes, each three qian; stewed rhubarb; licorice, each one qian. Chew well, boil with one cup of water, take before meals.[48p]

    　　加减三黄丸 【《千金翼》】 　治舌上黑，有数孔，出血如涌泉。　　戎盐　黄芩　黄蘗　大黄各五两　人参　桂心各二两　甘草一两，炙　　右七味末之，炼蜜丸如梧子，每服十丸，日三服；仍烧铁而烙之。

    　　定命散　治小儿缠喉，乳鹅等病。
    　　川大黄炒　黄连去须　直白僵蚕炒去丝嘴　生甘草各半两　五倍子一分　腻粉五筒子　　右为细末，每用一字，竹苇筒子吹入喉中。如毒气攻心，肺喉中生病，咽饮不得者，以乳汁调药一字，鸡羽蘸之，深探入喉中，得吐者活，不吐者死。[49p]

    Jia Jian San Huang Wan

    Used for treating black spots on the tongue, with several holes, and bleeding like a gushing spring. Ingredients: Each five taels of Rong salt, Huangqin (Scutellaria), Huangbo (Berberine), and Dahuang (Rhubarb); Each two taels of Ren shen (Ginseng) and Gui xin (Cinnamon heart); One tael of honey-roasted Gan cao (Licorice). Grind the seven ingredients into a powder, then prepare honeyed pills the size of a jujube. Take ten pills three times a day; also cauterize with iron.

    Tie Fen San

    Used to treat children's throat phlegm swelling. Ingredients: One fen of iron leaf powder, one fen of borax, and half a tael of raw alum. Grind into a powder; take half a qian mixed with cold water for two to three doses.

    She Tui San

    Used for throat phlegm swelling. Ingredients: One fen of snake skin, one fen of fried white plum flesh, half a tael of fried burdock seeds, and one fen of raw licorice. Grind into a powder; take one qian with a spoon, wrapping it in cotton and soaking it in soup for a short time, then having the child suck on it.

    Ding Ming San

    Used for treating children with obstruction in the throat from illnesses like lactating geese and similar conditions. Ingredients: Half a tael of fried Chuan Dahuang (Rhubarb), yellowing Huanglian (Coptis) after removing the beard, half a tael of fried Jiumai (Silkworm) with the mouth removed, half a tael of raw Gan cao (Licorice), one fen of Wubeishi (Galla chinensis), and five tubes of fatty powder. Grind into a fine powder; for each use, take a character's worth and blow it into the throat using a bamboo reed. If poison invades the heart, and the lung and throat are ill, and swallowing is not possible, mix the medicine with milk, dip a chicken feather in it, and deeply insert into the throat. If the patient throws up, they can be saved; if not, they will die.[49p]

    　　犀角散　治小儿马喉痹，其候如喉痹，更加连咽项颔颊肿甚，咽喉闭塞，但数数喷气，此证极恶。　　射干　桔梗各三分　马兰根一钱　甘草炙　川升麻　犀角屑各半两　　右为粗末，每服钱半，水一盏，入竹叶五片，煎至六分，去滓入马牙硝半钱，搅匀，细细含咽。
    　　绿云散　治小儿口疮，喉痹，马喉，鹅乳，重舌，木舌，一切咽喉之疾。　　螺青　盆硝　生蒲黄　生甘草各等分　　右为细末，每服一钱，生姜自然汁调，细细含咽。若已闭塞不通者，用苇筒入药吹入喉中。
    　　如圣汤　治咽喉一切诸疾。
    　　甘草二两　桔梗去芦，一两
    　　右为粗末，每服一大钱，水一盏，煎去滓，放温，时时呷，煎六分。
    　　龙石散　治同上。
    　　寒水石煅通赤，一分　朱砂研水飞，二分半　脑子研，半分　　右为细末，每用少许掺患处。病在咽喉者，吹入喉内，细细咽津，日五七次，临卧一两次用妙。[50p]

    Rhinoceros Horn Powder: Treats children with pharyngeal paralysis, presenting symptoms like pharyngeal paralysis, with additional swelling in the throat, neck, and cheeks, along with a feeling of obstruction in the throat, with only shallow breathing; this condition is extremely severe. Ingredients: Shegan, Platycodon (each three fen), Malan root (one qian), honey-fried Licorice, Chuan Shengma (each half liang), and Rhinoceros Horn shavings (each half liang). This is to be ground coarse. For each dose, take half a qian, add one cup of water, five pieces of bamboo leaves, and decoct until reduced to six parts, strain, add half a qian of Ma Ya Xie, mix well, and hold in the mouth to swallow slowly.

    Green Cloud Powder: Treats children's oral sores, pharyngeal paralysis, horse throat, goose milk symptoms, heavy tongue, wooden tongue, and all throat diseases. Ingredients: Luo Qing, pen salt, fresh cattail pollen, and fresh Licorice (all equal parts). This is to be ground finely. For each dose, take one qian, mix with the natural juice of fresh ginger, and hold in the mouth to swallow. If completely obstructed, use a reed tube to blow the medicine into the throat.

    Holy Decoction: Treats all diseases of the throat. Ingredients: Licorice (two liang), Platycodon (without its root, one liang). This is to be ground coarse. For each dose, take one large qian, add one cup of water, decoct and strain, allow to cool slightly, and sip occasionally until reduced to six parts.

    Dragon Stone Powder: Treats the same conditions as above. Ingredients: Calcinated cold water stone (one part), red mercury (two and a half parts), ground brain matter (half a part). This is to be ground finely. For each application, use a small amount to apply to the afflicted area. If the condition is in the throat, blow it inside the throat, slowly swallow the saliva, and repeat five to seven times a day, twice before sleeping for best results.[50p]

    　　如圣圆　治同上。
    　　川大黄末一分　白矾末一分　马屁勃末一分　蜗牛十四个　陈白梅肉十分　　右于五月五日午时取蜗牛，以白梅肉同研烂，入药和九如楝子大，每用一丸，绵裹含化咽津。若病重不能开口，即研药作末，苇筒吹入喉中，滴水三两点送之；或以净水磨药，灌之立瘥。

    Sanctified Formula
    For treatment, same as above.
    1 part ground yellow ochre, 1 part ground white alum, 1 part ground horse pelt, 14 snails, 10 parts dried white plum meat. On the fifth day of the fifth month at noon, take the snails, mix with the dried plum meat and grind them to a paste. Form into pills the size of jujube seeds; take one pill wrapped in cotton, let it dissolve in the mouth and swallow the saliva. If the illness is severe and the patient cannot open their mouth, grind the medicine into a powder, then blow it into the throat with a bamboo tube, using a few drops of water to help it down; or grind the medicine with clean water and administer it to ensure an immediate cure.

    Passage Formula
    For treatment, same as above.
    Dried white alum, water-ground realgar, lightly fried rhubarb, silkworms with heads removed, pig-tooth soappods with skin and strings removed. Grind each to a fine powder in equal parts; take a small amount and sniff it into the nose. In severe cases, blow it into the throat with a bamboo tube, leading to salivation or bleeding, causing an immediate cure.

    Golden Dew Ointment
    For treatment, same as above.
    Four ounces calcined cold water stone ground to a fine powder, one ounce realgar ground to a powder, two taels borax ground, and four taels licorice powder. Grind finely and mix well, then form into pills the size of tung seeds; dissolve one after meals.

    Shegan Decoction
    For treatment, same as above.
    One ounce shegan, one ounce Sichuan bulbus (wild black cohosh), half an ounce each of marrubium and horse pelt. Grind into a fine powder; take one qian, boil in one cup of water until reduced to six portions, strain and drink warm.[51p]

    Jingjie and Jiegeng Decoction treats sores in the throat.

    Jingjie spikes, dry stems with husks removed, fresh licorice, and roasted burdock seeds, all in equal portions. Grind to a fine powder. For each dose, use one qian with a small cup of water, decoct until reduced to six parts, strain and take warm.

    Another prescription for the same issue: Remove the husk from Jiegeng, fresh licorice, and roasted burdock seeds, each one liang. Grind to a coarse powder. For each dose, use one qian with a small cup of water, add a little bit of green salt, decoct until reduced to six parts, strain, let it cool, and sip occasionally.

    Another prescription for treating wind in the throat, causing obstruction: Char snake skin until it's yellow, and prepare Atractylodes (Duhuo) with husk removed and roasted, all in equal portions. Grind to a powder and take it with warm wine.

    Another prescription for the same issue: Remove the skin from two pieces of pigweed seeds, along with two qian of natron, grind to a powder and take with fresh water; if ineffective, take again.

    Another prescription for the same issue: Fresh Tian nanxing and raw white silkworms with the silk and mouth removed, each in equal portions. Grind to a powder, taking one character or half a qian with the natural juice of fresh ginger.

    For throat stagnation: Huangbai and cold water stone in equal portions. Grind to a powder, apply to the swollen area using peppermint water for medication, brushing it on with a chicken feather; if it dries, brush again.

    Another prescription for treating children's throat paralysis: Guixin and apricot kernels, each half liang.[52p]

    小儿唇口齿舌喉病门

    　　　　单方

    　　小儿紧唇：头垢涂之。 【《肘后方》】
    　　小儿唇紧：蛴螬研末，猪脂和敷之。 【《千金方》】　　又：松脂炙化贴之。 【《圣惠方》，下同】　　又：赤苋捣汁洗之，良。[53p]

    Right, mix these two ingredients into a powder, wrap it in cotton to the size of a jujube, and hold it in the mouth to swallow the saliva.

    Zhang Rui treats bleeding between the teeth.

    Boil bitter bamboo leaves in a strong concentration to extract the juice, adding a small amount of salt; when the temperature is suitable, let it cool and then spit it out.

    To unblock air, this remedy treats children who accidentally swallow coins or metallic objects stuck in the throat and not passable. Use one penny of goose feathers, ashes from burning them, a piece the size of a magnet, calcined, ground into fine powder. Add one part of burned ivory, preserving its essence. The above should be made into a fine powder; take half a penny each time, mix with fresh water, and swallow.

    The Great Sage’s Jade Flakes Worry-Free Powder treats all obstructions in the throat and all throat ailments, detoxifying and curing various diseases with immediate effect. Ingredients include: Yuan Shen, Guan Zhong, white poria fried until yellow, reduced sand cardamom, talc, jing jie, Shen Huang Lian after removing the hairs, mountain bean root, roasted licorice, borax, and cold water stone calcined and buried in earth to remove fire toxins, each three taels. Mix all into a powder; use half a penny each time, place in the mouth, and swallow with a mouthful of freshly drawn water.

    Children’s Remedies for Lip, Mouth, Tooth, Tongue, and Throat Diseases

    Single Formulas

    For tight lips in children: apply head dust. 【From "The Elbow Rear Recipe"】
    For tight lips in children: grind up larvae into a powder, mix with pig fat and apply. 【From "Thousand Gold Prescriptions"】 Another option: soften pine resin and apply. 【From "Holy Benefactor's Recipe," same as below】 Another: crush red amaranth, extract the juice and wash with it, good.[53p]

    　　小儿紧唇，脾热唇疮：并用乌蛇皮烧灰，酥和敷之。
    　　小儿肿唇：桑木汁涂之，即愈。

    　　小儿紧唇：葵根烧灰，酥调涂之。
    　　又：鸡矢白研末敷之，有涎易去。
    　　又：用马芥子捣汁曝浓，揩破频涂之。 【《崔氏纂要方》】　　又：人屎灰敷之。 【顾知悌方】
    　　又：用头垢枯矾研匀，猪胆调敷。 【《寿域》】
    　　小儿口疮：黄葵花烧末敷之。 【《肘后方》】
    　　治小儿口疮不得吮乳：用大青十八铢，黄连十二铢(口父)咀，以水三升，煮取一升二合，一服一合，日再夜一。 【《千金方》，下同】　　又：以蜜二升，甘草如指大三寸，腊月猪脂一斤，合煎相得，含如枣大，稍稍咽之，日三。　　又：以矾石如鸡子大置酢中，涂儿足下二七遍愈。
    　　治小儿燕口，两吻生疮：烧发灰和猪脂敷之。
    　　治小儿口下黄肌疮：取羖羊髭烧作灰，和腊月猪脂敷之；角亦可用。[54p]

    • For children with tight lips and heat sores: use ashes from black snake skin, mix with lard, and apply.

    • For children with swollen lips: apply mulberry wood juice, and it will heal.

    • For children with tight lips: use ashes from sunflower roots, mix with lard, and apply.

    • Additionally: grind white chicken droppings into a powder and apply it, which will help with drool.

    • Also: crush horse mustard seeds, extract the juice, concentrate it, and apply frequently.

    • Another remedy: use human feces ashes to apply.

    • Also: grind head grease with dry alum and mix with pig bile to apply.

    • For children's mouth sores: burn yellow hibiscus flowers into powder and apply.

    • To treat children's mouth sores that prevent them from nursing: use 18 zhu of Da Qing, 12 zhu of Huai Lian (for oral use), chew, and then boil in 3 sheng of water until it reduces to 1 sheng and 2 ge; take 1 ge each time, twice during the day and once at night.

    • Another remedy: use 2 sheng of honey, 3 inches of licorice, and 1 jin of winter pig fat; combine and cook, form pills the size of a date, and swallow a bit three times a day.

    • Additionally: place a piece of alum the size of an egg in vinegar and apply it to the child's feet for two to seven times until healed.

    • To treat children's candida (thrush) with sores on both sides of the lips: burn hair into ash and mix with pig fat to apply.

    • To treat children's yellow skin sores underneath the mouth: take the burned ash of ram's beard, mix with winter pig fat to apply; horns can also be used.[54p]

    　　治口傍恶疮：乱发灰、胡絮灰、黄连、干姜四味等分为散，以粉疮上，不过三遍。
    　　治小儿口中涎出：以白羊屎频内口中。　　又：以东行牛口中沫，涂口中及颐上；又桑白汁涂之瘥。
    　　小儿口紧，不能开口饮食，不语即死：蛇蜕烧灰，拭净敷之。
    　　治小儿鹅口，不能饮乳：用鹅屎汁沥儿口中。　　又：用黍米汁涂之。
    　　又：取小儿父母乱发净洗，缠桃枝，沾取井花水，东向向日中，以发拭口，得口中白乳，以置水中，七过沥洗，三朝作之。
    　　治小儿心热，口内生疮，重舌鹅口：用柘根銼五升，无根弓材亦佳，以水五升煎取二升，去滓煎取五合，细细服之，数次，良。
    　　治口疮白漫漫：先以父净发拭口，次取桑汁涂之。
    　　小儿流涎，胸膈有痰：新桑根白皮，捣自然汁，涂之甚效，干者煎水。 【《圣惠方》，下同】
    　　小儿鹅口，满口白烂：贝母去心为末半钱，水五分，蜜少许，煎三沸，缴净抹之，日四五度。[55p]

    Treatment for mouth sores: Mix equal parts of hair ash, downy hair ash, rhizoma coptidis, and dried ginger into a powder and apply to the sores no more than three times.

    For children with excessive salivation in the mouth: Use white sheep dung and apply it frequently inside their mouth. Additionally, use cow saliva from the east to coat the inside of the mouth and under the jaw; also, applying mulberry juice can aid in healing.

    For children with a tight mouth, unable to open for food or speak, leading to potential death: Burn snake skin into ash, clean thoroughly, and apply the ash.

    For children with oral thrush, unable to drink milk: Use the juice of goose droppings to rinse the child's mouth. Also, apply millet juice.

    Additionally: Take the father's clean hair, wash it, wrap it around a peach branch, dip it in well water, and facing east towards the sun, use the hair to wipe the mouth. If white fluid appears, place it in water, rinse it seven times, and repeat for three mornings.

    For children with heart heat causing mouth sores and a heavy tongue: Use five sheng of zhe roots, or bow wood without roots if preferable, boil with five sheng of water to extract two sheng, strain, then further boil to obtain five ge. Administer this finely, multiple times, for good results.

    To treat white, extensive mouth sores: First use the father's clean hair to wipe the mouth, then apply mulberry juice.

    For children drooling with phlegm in the chest: Use the white bark of new mulberry roots, crush to extract juice, apply it effectively; if dried, boil it in water.

    For children with oral thrush and a mouth full of white decay: Take half a qian of the heartless fritillary bulb, mix with five fen of water and a bit of honey, boil three times, strain and apply it four to five times a day.[55p]

    　　小儿吻疮，经年欲腐：葵根烧研敷之。
    　　小儿口噤，病在咽中，如麻豆许，令儿吐沫，不能乳食：葛蔓烧灰一字，和乳汁点之，即瘥。
    　　小儿鹅口重舌：甑带烧灰，敷舌下。
    　　小儿口疮：赤葵茎炙干为末，蜜和含之。
    　　燕口吻疮：胡粉炒一分，黄连半分，为末敷之。 【《普济方》，下同】
    　　小儿口疮：寒食面五钱，硝石七钱，水调半钱，涂足心，男左女右。　　又：用釜底墨，时时搽之。
    　　又：用大栗煮熟，日日与食之，甚效。
    　　小儿口疮糜烂：黄丹一钱，生蜜一两，相和蒸黑，每以鸡毛蘸搽甚效。
    　　小儿口疮及百日内口疮：用晚蚕蛾为末，入麝香少许掺之。
    　　小儿流涎脾热也。用鹿角屑末，米饮服一字。
    　　小儿鹅口，满口白烂：枯矾一钱，朱砂二分为末，每以少许傅之，日三次，神验。
    　　小儿流涎：用牛噍草绞汁，少少与之服。[56p]

    • For children with lip sores that have been festering for years: grind and apply burnt sunflower root.
    • For children who cannot speak due to throat illness, like a seed in the throat, make them spit; if they cannot eat: burn and grind kudzu vine ashes, mix with milk and apply, they will recover.
    • For children with a heavy tongue (oral thrush): apply ashes from a steaming pot beneath the tongue.
    • For children with mouth sores: dry and powder red sunflower stalks, mix with honey and have them suck on it.
    • For throat sores: fry one part of powdered honeysuckle with half a part of coptis and apply as a powder.
    • For mouth sores in children: use five qian of cold food flour, seven qian of nitre, and half qian of water for a paste to apply to the soles of the feet, left for boys and right for girls. Also, apply ink from the bottom of a pot regularly.
    • Additionally, boil large chestnuts until soft, and have them eat them daily, which is very effective.
    • For children with ulcerated mouth sores: mix one qian of yellow lead and one liang of raw honey, steam until black, and apply using a chicken feather, which is very effective.
    • For mouth sores in children and those within a hundred days: use the late silkworm moth powdered, mix with a little musk.
    • For children with drooling due to spleen heat: use powdered deer antler shavings, mixed with rice drink and have them take it.
    • For children with oral thrush and completely white mouths: use one qian of dried alum and two fen of cinnabar, grind to powder, apply a little three times a day, which is very effective.
    • For children who drool: squeeze juice from cattle straw and give a little to drink.[56p]

    　　小儿燕口，两角生疮：发灰三钱，饮汁服。 【《子母秘录》，下同】
    　　小儿口疮：五月五日虾蟆炙，研末敷之，即瘥。

    　　小儿口疮风疳：用柳木蛀虫屎烧存性为末，入麝香少许搽之；杂木亦可。 【《幼幼新书》】

    A child with sores in the mouth, two corners being affected: take three qian of powdered ash, mix with juice and administer.

    For a child's mouth sores: on the fifth day of the fifth month, roast a toad, grind it into powder and apply it, and it will heal.

    For a child's thrush: use mulberry bark juice mixed with white powder to apply.

    For a child's mouth sores: use roasted water chestnut, grind it into powder and mix it.

    Moreover, take equal parts of Coptis and aloe powder, take five fen with honey soup, for horse's ulcers, add toad ash in equal parts, reduce indigo by half, and a little musk.

    For a child’s mouth sores with wind ulcers: use the powder of burrowed wood insect feces burned to efficacy, mix in a little musk to apply; it can also be done with mixed wood.

    For a child's red mouth: apply light bamboo juice, or mix with breast milk.

    For a child with mouth sores who cannot suckle: mix powdered myrrh with vinegar and apply to the soles of the feet, wash away the sores once healed.

    In cases of severe mouth and nose ulcers threatening life in a few days: apply indigo paste thoroughly, ten times during the day and four times at night.

    For a child's recovering sores, mix powdered asarum and vinegar to apply on the belly button.[57p]

    　　治小儿口疮通白者，及风疳疮蚀透者：以白僵蚕炒令黄色，拭去蚕上黄肉毛为末，用蜜和敷之，去风热也。【《身经通考》方】
    　　小儿吻疮：竹沥和黄连、黄蘗、黄丹敷之。 【《全幼心鉴》】

    　　治小儿疳口疮：用天南星一　去皮为末，好酢调摊在纸上，男左女右，贴在脚心底，以帛系定，三日外取了，以温水洗尽脚下药。
    　　小儿鹅口、重舌、口疮：用青黛、(石卜)硝各一钱，片脑二分半，蜜调敷，仍视舌上有膜如榴子，则哭声不绝，随以指摘破即愈。【《幼幼近编》】
    　　小儿口疳：人中白煅、黄蘗蜜炙焦为末等分，入冰片少许，以青布拭净掺之。累效。 【《陆氏经验方》】
    　　小儿口疮：羊乳细滤入，含之数次愈。 【《小品方》】[58p]

    To treat children's oral ulcers that are white and those eroded by wind sores, fry white silkworms until yellow, wipe off the yellow flesh and hair, grind it into powder, and mix with honey to apply, which dispels wind heat.

    For children's lip sores, mix bamboo juice with yellow lian, yellow huang, and yellow dan to apply.

    For children's oral ulcers, use sheep fat decoction of coix root to apply.

    To treat red and white oral ulcers that occur after a child is startled, use one qian (a measurement) of raw alum to hold in the mouth; the stubborn saliva will reduce immediately.

    To treat children's malnutrition oral ulcers, use a piece of tian nanxing (a medicinal herb) peeled and ground into powder, mix with vinegar to spread on paper, place on the soles of the feet with the left for boys and right for girls, secure with cloth, and after three days, remove and wash the feet with warm water.

    For children's thrush, heavy tongue, and oral ulcers: use one qian each of indigo and (stone salt), two and a half fen of brain slices, mix with honey to apply. If there is a membrane like a pomegranate on the tongue, the crying will not cease; gently break it with a finger and it will heal.

    For children's oral malnutrition: mix equal parts of calcined bai dan (a type of medicinal powder) and yellow huang with honey, adding a small amount of ice powder, and use a blue cloth to wipe it clean to incorporate. Effective with repeated use.

    For children's oral ulcers: filter sheep's milk finely, hold in the mouth several times for healing.[58p]

    　　小儿鹅口：马牙硝擦舌上，日五度。 【《简要济众》】
    　　小儿口中白屑，名曰鹅口：用(石卜)硝、儿茶各二分，硼砂一分，为细末，用蜡叶捣自然汁，调搽儿口内，即安。并治马牙。【《穷乡便方》】
    　　小儿口疮痰烂：生硫黄水，调涂手心、足心，效即洗去。 【《危氏得效方》】
    　　小儿流涎，脾热有痰，皂荚子仁半两，半夏姜汤泡七次，一钱二分为末，姜汁丸麻子大，每水下五丸。【《圣济总录》】
    　　小儿口疮：铁锈末，水调敷之。 【《危氏集简方》，下同】
    　　婴孩鹅口，白厚如纸：用坯子胭脂，以乳汁调涂之，一宿效。男用女乳，女用男乳。
    　　小儿诸口疮：以香白芷、铜绿等分为末，掺上立效。 【《保幼大全》，下同】　　又：以白锡烧灰敷之。
    　　又：以汤瓶内碱为末，临卧时以好酢调于脚心底，明书个十字立验。
    　　治口气热臭：用干甜瓜子去壳研细，蜜少许，调成膏，食后含化，或敷齿上。[59p]

    • For children's oral thrush: Rub horse chestnut alkali on the tongue, five times a day.
    • For white flakes in children's mouths, known as oral thrush: Use two parts of vitriol and catechu, one part of borax, ground into a fine powder. Mix it with the juice from wax leaves to apply inside the mouth; this is effective. It also treats horse teeth.
    • For children with mouth sores and phlegm: Use fresh sulfur water to apply to the palms and soles; wash off if effective.
    • For children with excessive saliva, indicating heat and phlegm in the spleen: Use half a tael of soap pod seeds, soak in ginger decoction seven times, reduce to a powder of 1.2 qian, make ginger juice pills the size of sesame seeds, taking five pills with water.
    • For children's mouth sores: Use iron rust powder mixed with water as a poultice.
    • For infants with white oral thrush as thick as paper: Use a base of rouge mixed with milk and apply; effectiveness is seen overnight. Males use female milk, and females use male milk.
    • For various mouth sores in children: Grind fragrant white angelica and verdigris in equal parts; mix for immediate effect. Alternatively, use white tin ash as a poultice.
    • Also: Use ash from soda in a teapot, mixed with good vinegar, applied to the soles before sleeping, for effective results.
    • To treat bad breath with a hot odor: Use dried sweet melon seeds, shell and grind them fine, mix with a little honey to form a paste, which can be held in the mouth after eating, or applied to the teeth.[59p]

    　　小儿口舌病，小儿口疮，难用药：以天南星取中心，龙眼大为末，酢调涂儿脚心甚妙。【《医学纲目》，下同】　　又：用白矾或吴茱萸为末，酢调涂脚心，亦效。
    　　小儿口疮：黄蘗、青黛等分，片脑少许为末，竹沥调敷之。乳母宜服泻心汤、凉膈散。
    　　小儿口疮：用薄荷汁拭口内，西瓜水徐徐饮之。 【《入门》】
    　　治小儿齿落久不生：以牛屎中大豆二七枚，小开豆头，以注齿根处，数度即生。 【《千金方》，下同】　　又：取雄鼠屎二七枚，以一屎拭一齿根处，尽此上二十一日即生。雄鼠屎，两头尖者是。
    　　治牙齿根摇欲落：以生地黄大者一寸，绵裹着牙上，嚼咽汁，汁尽去之，日三即愈。可十日含之，更不发也。【《千金翼》，下同】
    　　治虫蚀齿根肉黑：烧腐棘，取沥涂之十遍，雄黄末敷即愈。若齿黑者，以松木灰揩之，细末雄黄涂龂百日，日再涂之。七日慎油猪肉，神效。[60p]

    For children's mouth diseases, such as sores that are difficult to treat with medicine: Take Tian Nan Xing (Arisaema) and grind it to a powder the size of a longan seed, mix with vinegar, and apply it to the soles of the child's feet - this is very effective.

    Additionally, using white alum or Wu Zhu Yu (Evodia) ground into powder, mix with vinegar and apply to the soles of the feet, which is also effective.

    For children's mouth sores: Mix equal parts of Huangbo (Phellodendron) and Qingdai (Indigo) with a small amount of powdered brain (a traditional ingredient) and apply with bamboo juice. Nursing mothers should take Xie Xin Tang and Liang Ge San.

    For mouth sores in children: Use mint juice to wipe the inside of the mouth, and drink watermelon juice slowly.

    To treat children whose teeth have fallen out and not grown back: Take 27 large soybeans from cow dung, split the soybean head, and insert it at the root of the tooth. After several applications, the teeth will grow.

    Alternatively: Take 27 pieces of male mouse droppings, use one dropping to wipe the root of each tooth; after doing this for twenty-one days, the teeth will grow back. The droppings of male mice should be pointed at both ends.

    To treat loose teeth about to fall out: Take one inch of fresh rhizome of Rehmannia (Sheng Di Huang), wrap it in cotton, place it on the tooth, chew, and swallow the juice; discard it after the juice is finished. Do this three times a day until healed, and you may hold it for ten days without further issues.

    To treat black rotten flesh at the tooth root: Burn the thorny plant (Fu Zhi), take the juice and apply it ten times, and apply powdered realgar to heal. If the tooth is black, wipe it with pine wood ash, apply finely powdered realgar on the gums for a hundred days, repeating twice daily. For seven days, avoid oily pork for a divine effect.[60p]

    　　治小儿齿龋：切白马悬蹄可孔，塞之，不过三度。
    　　治虫蚀齿疼痛闭气，细书曰：南方赤头虫，飞来入某姓名裂齿里，今得蝎虫孔，安置耐居上，急急如律令！小笺纸内，若屋柱北边蝎虫孔中，取水一杯，禹步如禁法，还诵上文，以水沃孔，以净黄土泥之，勿令泄气，永愈。
    　　小儿齿迟：正旦取尿坑中竹木刮涂之，即生。 【《圣惠方》，下同】　　一：取路旁遗却稻粒，于齿路点三七下，其齿自生，神效。
    　　小儿牙疳出血：大鲫鱼一尾，去肠留鳞，入当归末泥固烧存性，入煅过盐和匀，日用。
    　　小儿齿痛：以皂荚炙去皮子捣未，取少许，着齿痛上瘥。
    　　小儿龋齿：以松柏脂捏锐如锥，柱龋孔内，须臾龋虫缘松脂出，即差。
    　　小儿牙疳：雄黄一钱，铜绿二钱为末贴之。 【《陈氏小儿方》】[61p]

    Treatment for children's tooth decay: Cut a piece of white horse hoof into holes, plug them, and repeat no more than three times.

    For pain due to worm-eaten teeth, it is written: A red-headed worm from the South flies in and enters a person's cracked tooth. Now, obtain a scorpion's hole and place it above, urgently and according to the law! Inside a small note, if it’s from the scorpion's hole on the north side of a building pillar, take a cup of water, walk according to the restricted method, and recite the above text. Water the hole and fill it with clean yellow earth mud to prevent any air leakage for everlasting recovery.

    For late-emerging children's teeth: On New Year's Day, scrape bamboo from a urinal and apply it to the teeth; they will grow as if by magic.

    For children's bleeding gums: One large crucian carp, remove the intestines but keep the scales, mix with powdered angelica and clay, solidify it by burning; then combine it with pre-cooked salt and use daily.

    For children's toothache: Roast soap pods, remove the skins, grind them, take a small amount and apply it to the painful teeth.

    For children's cavities: Knead cedar sap until it is sharp like a needle and place it into the cavity. The cavity will heal quickly as the decay is drawn out alongside the cedar sap.

    For children's gum disease: One pennyweight of realgar and two pennyweights of verdigris, ground into a powder and applied as a paste.[61p]

    　　一以鼋胆少许，生姜薄荷汁化服，得吐便愈。
    　　一青鱼胆亦得，收得以青黛酿之。

    　　小儿缠喉风，束气不通：以白僵蚕二个去丝为末，生姜自然汁调，更入蜜少许拌匀，分二三服，或只用半钱一字，旋调服之。
    　　缠喉、乳鹅、喉痹、咽喉、颔项，肿闷闭塞，气不得通者：令患人先呷好麻油少许，后以茶叶烧灰，细末，水调下半钱，立效。大者增之。　　一方：以马衔一具，水二盏煎至半，量大小分服。
    　　治悬痈忽倒：以白矾灰盐各半两研细，箸头点上拨正；亦治肿闷，日七八遍。
    　　治咽喉腮颊肿闷：以蒜塞耳鼻中。
    　　又：以马鞭草根截去两头，取在中者，捣汁服之。
    　　小儿咽喉肿塞闷：以桑上螳螂窠一两烧灰，马屁勃半两，同研匀细。炼蜜丸桐子大，三岁煎犀角汤研下三圆。大者加之。[70p]

    If a child has a throat membrane disease and cannot speak, boil soybean juice, let it cool, and have them hold it in their mouth.

    For an additional remedy, take a small amount of turtle bile and mix it with ginger and mint juice to consume; this can cause vomiting and lead to recovery. Another option is to use the gallbladder of a blue fish, prepared with indigo.

    For children suffering from wind in the throat, which constricts breathing: take two silkworms (without their silk) and grind them into a powder, mix it with natural ginger juice and a little honey, and divide it into two or three doses, or use half a coin-sized amount and adjust as needed.

    For throat constriction, tender throat, throat membrane disease, and swelling that causes suffocation and obstructs breathing: have the patient first take a small amount of good sesame oil, then use tea leaves burned to ash, grind finely, and mix it with water to take half a coin's worth, producing immediate effects. For larger patients, increase the dosage. Another method is to use a horse's bridle, boil it with two cups of water until reduced by half, and then administer according to size.

    To treat sudden abscesses, mix half an ounce each of alum, ash, and salt, grind finely, and apply it with a chopstick tip; this also treats swelling and can be applied seven to eight times a day.

    For swelling in the throat, cheeks, and discomfort: insert garlic into the ears and nose. Additionally, take the root of verbena, cut off both ends, and use the middle part to extract the juice for consumption.

    For a child with a swollen and obstructed throat: burn one ounce of mantis nest collected from mulberry trees and mix it with half an ounce of horse's tail, grinding them together finely. Form into pills the size of a tung seed, and for children around three years old, grind and mix with rhinoceros horn soup in three circles; increase dosage for older children.[70p]

    　　小儿饮乳不快，觉似喉痹：以沙牛角烧刮取灰，涂乳上吮儿，咽下即差。
    　　治小儿悞吞针刺喉中：以磁石如枣核大，磨令光钻作窍子，以线穿系定，令儿含之，针则自出。若悞吞钱者，用枣大。治悞吞竹木入喉，烧秤锤通赤，渍酒饮之。
    　　治悞吞金银铜铁钱物，在喉中不下：以南天烛根烧灰研细，熟水调服一钱，立下。
    　　治悞吞金银铜铁钱等物，在腹内不下：以石灰一皂子许，硫黄半皂子许，同研为末，酒服之。　　又：以胡粉一两，水调分服，量大小加减。
    　　治鱼骨鲠喉不下：以硇砂少许，口中咀嚼，咽之立下。又以故鱼网覆颈项，则下；未可，煮汁饮之立下。　　又：以鸬鹚毛烧灰，水调服，量大小与。
    　　冶一切诸般骨刺，竹木签刺，梗喉不下：于腊月取鳜鱼胆，北檐下阴干，每用少许，酒煎化温呷，得逆便吐，梗乃随出。未吐再服。其梗刺虽咽在腹内，久痛黄瘦者，服之亦出，极妙。无鳜鱼，取青鱼鲤蠡鱼胆亦可。并治喉痹。[71p]

    Children who are slow to drink milk may feel like they have a throat obstruction: Take sand cowhorn, burn it and scrape to obtain ash, apply it to the milk for the child to suck, and swallowing will resolve the issue.

    For children who accidentally swallow a needle stuck in the throat: Use a magnet the size of a jujube, polish it until smooth and drill a small hole, attach a thread to it, and have the child hold it in their mouth; the needle will then come out. If the child swallows money, use a piece the size of a jujube. To treat swallowing bamboo or wood lodged in the throat, burn a weight hammer until it glows red, soak it in wine and drink.

    For swallowing gold, silver, copper, iron coins, or similar objects, lodged in the throat and not going down: Burn the root of the southern candle and grind the ash fine, mix with warm water and take one qian, and it will go down immediately.

    For swallowing gold, silver, copper, iron coins, etc., lodged in the belly and not going down: Mix one “zhao” of lime with half a “zhao” of sulfur and grind into powder, take with wine. Alternatively: Take one liang of hui powder, mix with water and divide into doses, adjusting according to size.

    For a fish bone stuck in the throat: Take a small amount of calamine, chew in the mouth, and swallow; it will go down immediately. Alternatively, cover the neck with an old fish net to help it go down; if that doesn't work, boil it in juice and drink it to help it go down. Also: use cormorant feathers burnt to ash, mix with water and take, adjusting for size.

    To treat all sorts of bone splinters, bamboo or wooden splinters stuck in the throat: In the twelfth month, take the gallbladder of a mandarin fish, dry it in the shade under the north eave; use a small amount, stew it in wine until melted and warm, sip it and the foreign object will come out, continue taking if not expelled. Even if the splinter remains in the belly and causes long-term pain and yellowing, taking this will also help it come out, which is extremely effective. If mandarin fish is not available, the gallbladder of a carp or catfish can also work, and it also treats throat obstructions.[71p]

    　　治桃李果梗：以狗头煮汤摩头上。

    　　　　针灸

    　　《千金方》曰：小儿重舌，灸行间随年壮。穴在足大趾岐中。又灸两足外踝上三壮。　　《古今医统》曰：小儿乳鹅，针少商一分，灸则一壮。少商在大指端内侧，去爪甲角如韭叶，白肉际宛宛中，肺脉所出，为井木。单乳鹅针合谷三分，灸则三壮。合谷一名虎口，手大指次指岐骨间陷中，手阳明大肠脉所过为原。　　小儿五六岁不语者，心气不足，舌本无力，发转难，灸心俞穴三壮，在五椎下两旁各一寸半陷中。　　小儿急喉痹，天突穴一穴，灸一壮，在结喉下三寸。　　《幼幼近编》曰：凡小儿患喉蛾，急以银针挑破发顶上，出血即愈。[72p]

    To treat peach and plum fruit obstruction: Use dog's head to boil soup and apply it to the top.

    To treat various obstructions in the throat: Use powdered mullein, mix with half a qian or one qian of water to take.

    To treat all kinds of beads, earrings, coins, and similar items stuck in the throat: Burn a copper bow to red heat, place it in water, and let the cool water be taken.

    Acupuncture and Moxibustion

    The "Thousand Gold Prescriptions" states: For children with a heavy tongue, moxibustion should be applied along the interspaces according to their growth. The acupoint is in the middle of the big toe’s joint. Additionally, moxibustion should be applied at three points above the outer ankle of both feet. The "Medical Regulations of Ancient and Modern" states: For children with a milk hiccup, use a needle to prick the Shaoshang point for one fen, followed by moxibustion for one bunch. Shaoshang is on the inner side of the tip of the big toe, one should avoid the nail edge like chives, locating it at the white flesh, where the lung meridian emerges, called Jingmu. For a milk hiccup, needle the Hegu point for three fen, followed by moxibustion for three bunches. Hegu, also known as the Tiger's Mouth, is found in the depression between the first and second metacarpal bones of the hand, where the Yangming large intestine meridian runs through.

    For children aged five to six who do not speak, it indicates insufficient heart energy; the root of the tongue lacks strength, causing difficulty in articulation. Moxibustion should be applied to the Xinshu point for three bunches, located one and a half inches lateral to the two sides below the fifth vertebra. For children with acute throat obstruction, moxibustion should be applied to the Tiantu point for one bunch, located three inches below the Adam's apple. The "Young Children’s Compendium" states: If a child suffers from throat worms, use a silver needle to puncture the top of the head; once blood flows, they will recover.[72p]

    　　　　医案

    　　万氏《幼科发挥》曰：一儿患口舌生疮，医用药服之搽之者，皆芩、连、知、药类，无效。予曰：心热所为。苦入心而反助其热，宜无效。乃作洗心散与之，一服而安。
    　　予甥满口生疮，咽喉唇舌皆是。予用蘗、连一钱，朱砂、白矾五分，鼠妇焙干三分，共为研细敷之，立效，乃奇方也。
    　　《薛氏医案》曰：一小儿弄舌发搐，手指不冷，余谓肝脾虚热，用异功散加升麻、柴胡而愈。后伤乳腹胀，服克伐作泻，弄舌手指发热。审乳母肝火，与小柴胡汤加升麻、白朮治之，母子并愈。
    　　一小儿乳食过多，患吐泻，用大剂异功散加柴胡、升麻，母子服之而愈。后因惊服至宝丹之类，发搐弄舌，几至慢惊，余用六君子汤加白附子服之而愈。[73p]

    Medical Case Record

    The Wan family's "Pediatric Exploration" states: A child suffers from sores on the mouth and tongue. The doctor prescribed various medications containing Scutellaria, Coptis, and other similar drugs, to no effect. I said this is caused by heat in the heart. Bitter herbs enter the heart and further support its heat, hence they are ineffective. I then formulated a "Heart-Cleansing Powder," and after one dose, the child was calm.

    My nephew had sores all around his mouth, affecting the throat, lips, and tongue. I used one qian of Herba Coptidis and Radix Scutellariae, five fen of vermilion and white alum, and three fen of roasted pill millipede, ground them finely, and applied it as a poultice. It worked immediately; this is indeed a marvelous remedy.

    The "Xue Family Medical Records" states: A small child played with his tongue and had convulsions; his fingers were not cold. I diagnosed this as a deficiency of liver and spleen with heat, treated with a modified Yigong Powder combined with Cimicifuga and Bupleurum, leading to recovery. Later, he suffered from abdominal distention after feeding on milk; when treated with a purgative, he exhibited convulsions again. After checking the wet nurse, who had excessive liver fire, I used Xiao Chai Hu Decoction with added Cimicifuga and Atractylodes, and both mother and child recovered.

    Another small child, having consumed too much milk, experienced vomiting and diarrhea. I prescribed a large dose of Yigong Powder with added Bupleurum and Cimicifuga, and both mother and child recovered. Later, due to fright, he took several precious pills, which caused convulsions and tongue movements, nearly leading to chronic convulsions. I then administered Liu Junzi Decoction with added Aconitum and he recovered.[73p]

    　　一小儿吐舌，发热饮冷，额鼻黄赤，吐舌流涎，余谓心脾实热，用导赤泻黄二散而愈。后复作，别服清热等药，更弄舌，余用异功散加钓藤钩而安，又用六君子汤全愈。
    　　《证治准绳》曰：一小儿喉间肿痛，惊悸，饮水，服惊风降火之药益甚。他医仍欲攻风痰。余曰：惊悸饮水，心经虚证。盖胃为五脏之本。先用五味异功散以补胃，加桔梗、甘草以消毒，诸证顿退；后用牛蒡子汤加柴胡而愈。
    　　一小儿发热饮冷，大便黄色，手足并热，不能吮乳。视口内无患，们其喉间则哭。此喉内作痛，乃脾胃实热也。用泻黄、清胃二散各一剂，母子并服而愈。后因乳母饮酒，儿躁不安，口内流涎。仍用前二散而愈。
    　　一小儿喉间肿痛，发热咳嗽，大便秘结，此肝与大肠有热，先用牛蒡子汤加硝、黄一服，大便随通；乃去硝黄，再剂顿愈。审其母有肝火发热，用柴胡清肝散，母子并服而痊。[74p]

    A young child sticks out his tongue, has a fever, drinks cold water, his forehead and nose are yellow and red, he sticks out his tongue and drools. I believed it was due to excessive heat in the heart and spleen, and treated him with the "Yao Chi" and "Xie Huang" powders, resulting in recovery. Later, he had a relapse, and I prescribed other cooling medicines. Examining his tongue again, I used "Yi Gong San" with added "Diao Teng Gou," and he was at ease; subsequently, I used "Liu Jun Zi Tang" to achieve complete recovery.

    In the "Zheng Zhi Zhun Sheng," it is stated: A young child has swelling and pain in the throat, experiences fright and anxiety, and drinking water and taking medications for convulsions and reducing heat worsens his condition. Other doctors insisted on attacking wind phlegm. I reasoned that the fright and anxiety indicated a deficiency in the heart. Indeed, the stomach is the root of the five organs. First, I used "Wu Wei Yi Gong San" to nourish the stomach, adding "Jie Geng" and "Gan Cao" to clear toxins, and all symptoms immediately subsided; then I prescribed "Niu Bang Zi Tang" with added "Chai Hu," resulting in recovery.

    A young child experiences fever, drinks cold water, has yellow stools, and both hands and feet feel hot, making it impossible for him to suckle. Upon inspection, there were no issues in the mouth, but he cried when examining his throat. The pain in his throat was due to excessive heat in the spleen and stomach. I used "Xie Huang" and "Qing Wei" powders, with both mother and child taking a dose, resulting in recovery. Later, due to the wet nurse consuming alcohol, the child became restless and drooled. I again used the previous two powders, leading to recovery.

    A young child has swelling and pain in the throat, along with fever and cough, and suffers from constipation. This indicates heat in both the liver and the large intestine. First, I used "Niu Bang Zi Tang" with added "Niao" and "Huang," and bowel movements were immediately facilitated; then, removing the "Niao" and "Huang," he recovered with a subsequent dose. Noticing that the mother had excessive liver heat, I used "Chai Hu Qing Gan San," and both mother and child recovered completely.[74p]

    　　《薛氏医案》曰：一小儿喉肿作渴，大便干实，右腮赤色，此肺与大肠经实热也。用柴胡饮子一服而愈。后因饮食停滞，服峻厉之药，喉间仍肿，腹中胀痛，此脾气复伤也，用异功散加升麻、当归而痊。
    　　一小儿因母忿怒，患前证，兼咬牙呵欠，余谓肝经虚热之证，子用甘桔汤加柴胡、山栀、牛蒡子，母服加味逍遥散而愈。
    　　一小儿嗜膏梁之味，喉间肿痛，痰涎壅盛，服巴豆丸，前证益甚，口鼻出血，唇舌生疮，大便不实。余用犀角地黄汤解膏粱之热，用东垣安胃散解巴豆之毒，又用桔梗汤而愈。
    　　一小儿喉间肿痛，左腮色青赤，此心肝二经之热也，用柴胡清肝散而愈。后因惊服至宝丹，吐痰发搐，手足指冷，此肝木虚而肺金乘之，用补中益气汤以补脾肺，六味地黄丸以滋肝肾而痊。
    　　一小儿额间赤，足心热，喉中常痛，服清胃败毒之药，余谓禀肾水不足，而心火炽甚也，当用地黄丸壮水之主以制阳光。不悟，口舌赤烈，小便如淋而殁。[75p]

    The "Medical Cases of the Xue Family" states: A young child had throat swelling with thirst, dry and hard stools, and a red right cheek; this indicated excess heat in the lung and large intestine channels.     　　一小儿喉间肿痛，口角流涎，手足并热，用泻黄、清胃二散，母子服之而愈。后因母大怒，儿憎寒发热，仍复流涎，用柴胡清肝散加漏芦，母子服之而愈。
    　　一女子六岁，喉间肿痛，鼻中息肉，寒热往来，小便频数，良久变白，此肝疳之证，先用加味逍遥散加炒黑焦龙胆草，热痒渐退；乃去龙胆草，佐以四味肥儿丸而愈。
    　　　小儿胸背手足病门

    　　　　小儿直诀 【宋、钱乙】

    　　　　　龟胸龟背

    　　龟胸龟背者，由儿生下风客于脊，入于骨髓，致成龟背；若肺热胀满，攻于胸膈，即成龟胸。并用龟尿点其骨节自愈。其取尿法，用青莲叶安龟在上，用镜照之，其尿自出。　　 【注　按小儿元气未充，腠理不密，风邪乘之；或痰饮蕴热于肺，风热交攻而致；或坐早风入骨髓。治当调补脾肺为主。若因乳母厚味辛辣而致者，当兼治其母。若因禀父肝肾虚热者，用六味地黄丸。若禀肾气不足者，用八味地黄丸。】
    　　　　　行迟[76p]

    A young child had swelling and pain in the throat, drooling from the corners of the mouth, and warmth in the hands and feet. By taking the “Purge Yellow” and “Clear Stomach” powders, both mother and child were cured. Later, due to the mother’s great anger, the child developed chills and fever again, and continued to drool. They used Chai Hu Qing Gan San with added Lo Hu, and both were cured.

    A six-year-old girl had swelling and pain in the throat, nasal polyps, alternating chills and fever, and frequent urination that eventually turned white. This was a symptom of liver dampness. At first, she was treated with an enhanced version of Xiao Yao San with fried black and charred gentian root, which gradually alleviated the heat and itching. Then the gentian root was removed, and four kinds of Fei Er Wan were used to achieve a cure.

    Children's diseases of the chest and back.

    Children's Due Treatise [by Qian Yi of the Song Dynasty]

    “Curved Chest and Curved Back”

    Curved chest and curved back occur when a child is afflicted by wind that invades the spine and enters the marrow, resulting in a curved back. If there is lung heat and fullness attacking the chest and diaphragm, it leads to a curved chest. Use turtle urine to apply to the joints for self-healing. The method of obtaining the urine involves placing a tortoise on blue lotus leaves and using a mirror to reflect it, causing the urine to flow out.

    [Note: A child's vital energy is not fully developed, and their skin pores are not tightly sealed, allowing wind evil to penetrate. Alternatively, phlegm and heat can accumulate in the lungs, hence the attack of wind and heat leading to these symptoms; or the child may have been exposed to wind too early, resulting in the invasion into the marrow. Treatment should primarily focus on nourishing the spleen and lungs. If the condition arises due to the mother’s consumption of rich and spicy foods, her treatment should also be addressed. If it is due to constitutional deficiency of the father's liver and kidney heat, Liu Wei Di Huang Wan should be used. If it is due to a deficiency of kidney qi, Ba Wei Di Huang Wan should be used.]

    Delayed action.[76p]

    　　长大不行，行则脚软，胎弱也。
    　　【注　小儿行迟：有肝肾虚，长而不能行者；有肝气虚而手足拳挛者；有肝肾虚而脚不能舒展者。并用地黄丸滋补之。】
    　　　　片玉心书 【明　万全】

    　　　　　龟胸龟背

    　　龟胸者，其胸高肿，状如龟样，此肺热也。加减葶苈丸主之。　　小儿龟胸证，肺热胀于胸，加减葶苈丸服之，有神功。龟背者，坐卧伛偻，状如龟背，由客风吹脊入于骨髓，此证多成痼疾。间有灸肺俞二穴第三椎骨节下两傍各寸半，膈俞穴第二骨下两傍各寸半，如此而收功者，然未尽见效也。以枳壳丸主之。　　龟背为恶证，肾风入骨髓。内服枳壳丸，灸法宜相继。
    　　　　　行迟

    　　行迟者何也？盖骨乃髓之所养，血气不充则髓不满骨，故弱软不能行。此由肾与肝俱虚得之。盖肝主筋，筋弱而不能早行；肾主骨，骨弱而不坚。加味地黄丸主之。　　肝肾两虚行不足，肝主筋兮肾主骨。若要二经气血充，加味地黄能助补。[77p]

    When a child fails to grow, or if they are able to walk but their legs are weak, it indicates a deficiency of the胎 (prenatal essence).

    Children who walk late may have deficient liver and kidney, and those who are unable to walk as they grow may also have this condition; some may exhibit weakness in their liver qi and experience cramps in their hands and feet. If the liver and kidneys are both weak, they cannot extend their legs. The remedy is to use the Rehmannia Six Formula for nourishment.

    The condition of "turtle chest" refers to a swollen, elevated chest that resembles a turtle, indicating lung heat. This can be treated with a modified Gengzhi Pill. In the case of children with turtle chest due to lung heat, administering this modified formula can bring about miraculous results.

    The condition of "turtle back" presents as a hunched posture resembling a turtle shell, which is caused by external wind affecting the spine and entering the marrow. This often leads to a chronic ailment. Moxibustion should be applied to the two points next to the third vertebra and the two points next to the second vertebra, one and a half cun away from the spine. While this method works, it may not always yield results. The Zhiqiao Pill should be used. Turtle back is a severe condition marked by kidney wind entering the marrow. Internal consumption of the Zhiqiao Pill and moxibustion should be done consecutively.

    What is meant by walking late? Bones are nourished by marrow, and if blood and qi do not sufficiently fill the marrow, the bones become weak and soft, leading to an inability to walk. This arises from both kidney and liver deficiency. Since the liver governs the tendons, weakness in the tendons prevents early walking; the kidney governs the bones, and weak bones cannot be strong. The remedy is to use the modified Rehmannia Six Formula.

    When both the liver and kidney are deficient, leading to inadequate walking capability, since the liver governs tendons and the kidney governs bones, replenishing the qi and blood of both meridians can be achieved by using the modified Rehmannia formula for assistance.[77p]

    　　　　　鹤膝

    　　脚细者禀受不足，气血不充，故肌肉瘦薄，骨节俱露，如鹤之膝。此亦由肾虚，名鹤膝节。加味地黄丸主之。　　小儿鹤膝，此属肾虚。地黄加味。服却无虞。
    　　　　婴童百问 【明　鲁伯嗣】

    　　　　　龟背龟胸鹤膝行迟

    　　《圣惠》论：小儿龟胸者，缘肺热气胀满而成此疾；乳母多食辛辣之物，亦成此候；或乳母有宿乳，乳儿亦成此疾。常捏去宿乳，则无此证也。当用圣惠龟胸丸治之。　　《圣惠》论：龟背者，小儿初生未满半周，强令早坐，逐使客风吹脊，故令背高如龟之状也，有灸法可疗。　　又有鹤膝证，钱氏地黄丸加鹿茸以补肾气。　　又有行迟之证，地黄丸加牛膝、五加皮、补骨脂、及酒炙鹿茸，又有五加皮散治之。　　又治龟首，有龟胸丸以散其热。松蕊丹、百合丹，治龟胸龟背尤佳。羚羊角丸治五六岁不能行走。[78p]

    Crane Knee

This is also due to kidney deficiency, named crane knee joint. Modified Rehmannia Pills are the remedy for this. For children with crane knee, this is associated with kidney deficiency.     Turtle Back, Turtle Chest, Crane Knee, and Delayed Walking

    　　　　　龟胸龟背

    　　　　　鹤膝风

    Babies' Essentials
    Ming Dynasty, Xue Kai

    Turtle Chest and Turtle Back

    The condition known as "Turtle Chest and Turtle Back" primarily requires the adjustment and supplementation of the spleen and lungs, with an addition of clearing heat and resolving phlegm.     Crane Knee Wind

    "Crane Knee Wind" refers to legs that are thin, with knees that are thicker, resembling a crane's knee, hence the name. This condition arises from insufficient kidney energy, allowing external pathogens to invade. Initially, there is pain inside the knee, with no change in external color, and difficulty in bending or stretching. If within one or two months it swells, turns red, and produces pus, it can be treated; if it is hard, white, and does not produce pus, it is difficult to treat. For early cases, use "Major Fangfeng Decoction" as the main remedy, supplementary with "Qi-boosting and Nourishing Decoction"; for advanced cases, use "Middle Qi Tonifying Decoction" with "Major Fangfeng Decoction" as a supplement, and be cautious not to use drugs that promote qi dispersal. If not resolved or if symptoms like fever appear, the spleen and stomach should be adjusted and supplemented well; otherwise, it will definitely worsen.

    　　　　尊生书

    　　　　　龟胸

    　　龟胸乃肺热胀满，有痰成之。忌破气发散，肺虚也；亦忌收濇，宜降气消痰。
    　　　　证治准绳 【明　王肯堂】

    　　　　　龟胸

    　　张氏云：乳母乳儿，常捏去宿乳；夏常洗乳净，捏去热乳。若令儿饮热乳，损伤肺气，胸高胀满，令儿胸高如龟，乃名龟胸。　　曾氏云：此候因风痰停饮，聚积心胸，再感风热。肺为诸脏华盖，居于膈上，水气泛溢，则肺为之浮，日久凝而为痰，停滞心胸，兼以风热内发，其外证唇红面赤，咳嗽喘促，致胸骨高如覆掌，名曰龟胸。治法宽肺化痰利膈，以除肺经痰饮。先用五苓散和宽气饮，入姜汁葱汤调服；次清肺饮、雄黄散、碧玉丸、如意膏为治。若投前药愈而复作，传变目睛直视，痰涎上涌，兼以发搐，则难治矣。
    　　　　　龟背

    　　坐儿稍早，为客风吹脊，风气达髓，使背高如龟。虽有药方，多成痼疾，以灸法为要。在百日内不治。[80p]

    Respecting Life Focus

    Turtle Chest

    The condition known as Turtle Chest is due to heat in the lungs causing fullness, which results in phlegm. It is advised to avoid breaking up the qi and dispersing it, as this may weaken the lungs; instead, one should avoid retention and seek to descend qi and eliminate phlegm.

    Standard for Diagnosis and Treatment [Ming Dynasty, Wang Kengtang]

    Turtle Chest

    According to Zhang, if a wet nurse feeds an infant, it is common to squeeze out any stagnant milk; in summer, it is important to wash the milk clean and squeeze out the hot milk. Allowing the infant to drink hot milk can damage lung qi, leading to a swelling and fullness in the chest, which can make the chest rise high like a turtle, hence the name Turtle Chest. According to Zeng, this condition arises from wind and phlegm accumulating in the heart and chest, and subsequently, from exposure to wind and heat. The lungs, being the canopy of all organs, reside above the diaphragm. If water and qi overflow, the lungs become distended and, over time, solidify into phlegm, stagnating in the heart and chest. When compounded by internal wind and heat, external symptoms manifest as red lips and a flushed face, accompanied by cough and shortness of breath, causing the sternum to rise as if covered by a palm, termed Turtle Chest. The method of treatment is to relax the lungs, transform phlegm, and benefit the diaphragm to eliminate phlegm from the lung meridian. Initially, one should use the Wuling Powder mixed with a soothing qi decoction, combined with ginger juice and scallion broth for administration; next, utilize Qingfei Decoction, Xionghuang Powder, Biyu Pills, and Ruyi Ointment for treatment. If the initial medicine cures the condition but it recurs, if the transformation directs phlegm and saliva upwards, combined with seizures, it becomes difficult to treat.

    Turtle Back

    If the child sits up too early and windy conditions affect the spine, the wind can reach the marrow, causing the back to elevate like a turtle. Although there are many prescriptions, they often become chronic ailments, and moxibustion is crucial. It should be treated within the first hundred days.[80p]

    　　　　　行迟

    　　张氏云：凡儿生至周岁三百六十日，膝骨成，乃能行。近世小儿多因父母气血不足，故令胎气不强，骨气软弱，筋脉无力，不能行步。鹿茸丹主之，曾经大效。　　汤氏云：小儿不能行，治法当用钱氏补肾地黄丸加鹿茸、五加皮、麝香。外甥黄知录之子，三岁不能行，遂合此方服之，有验。
    　　　　医学入门 【明　李梴】

    　　　　　手足

    　　手软，无力以动也。所受肝弱，两手筋缩不能舒伸。薏苡丸主之。　　脚软行迟，乃骨髓不满，气血不充，筋弱不能束骨。宜肾气丸加牛膝、五加皮、鹿茸。五六岁不行者，羊角丸；三岁不能行者，用五加皮一两、牛膝、木瓜各五钱为末，每二钱，米饮入酒少许，调服。有脚指蜷缩无力，不能展伸者，海桐散主之。有鹤节风，俗云鼓捶风，乃肾虚精髓内耗，为风邪所袭，皮肤不荣，日渐枯瘁，如鹤脚之节。宜肾气丸加五加皮、鹿茸、牛膝。[81p]

    Delayed Walking

    Zhang said: Generally, a child must reach three hundred sixty days old, with knee bones formed, before they can walk. In recent times, many children are unable to walk due to their parents' insufficient vitality and blood, which weakens the fetal energy, resulting in weak bones and muscles, making it impossible to take steps. The use of deer antler has proven effective. Tang stated that for children who cannot walk, the treatment should utilize Qian's Kidney Tonic with Rehmannia pills, adding deer antler, bark of Wu Jia, and musk. My nephew Huang Zhiluo's son could not walk at three years old; after taking this recipe, it yielded results.

    Medicine for Beginners (Ming Era, Li Zhan)

    Hands and Feet

    Weak hands cannot move effectively. This results from weak liver, causing the tendons in both hands to retract without being able to extend. The treatment is Yi Yi Wan. Weak and slow-moving feet signify insufficient bone marrow, inadequate qi and blood, and weak tendons that cannot support the bones. The remedy should be Kidney Qi Pills combined with Niu Xi, Wu Jia Pei, and deer antler. For those who cannot walk at five or six years old, sheep horn pills are recommended; for those unable to walk by three years old, use one tael of Wu Jia Pei, five qian each of Niu Xi and Mu Guo, ground into powder, and taken with a small amount of rice drink mixed with a bit of alcohol. For toes that curl and lack strength to extend, the remedy is Hai Tong San. Cases of "crane joints wind," commonly known as "drumstick wind," arise from kidney deficiency and depletion of essence, being attacked by wind evil. This leads to the skin not being nourished, gradually becoming withered, like a crane's joint. The suitable treatment is Kidney Qi Pills combined with Wu Jia Pei, deer antler, and Niu Xi.[81p]

    　　　　　龟胸

    　　肺经受热，故胸高肿满，状似龟胸也。轻则泻白散加山栀、天门冬，甚则百合丹。切禁五辛酒面炙煿煎炒之物。

    Young Guides

    Turtle Chest

    When the lung meridian is heated, the chest swells high and is full, resembling a turtle's chest. For mild cases, administer Xie Bai San with Shan Zhi and Tian Men Dong; for severe cases, use Bai He Dan. Strictly avoid foods that are pungent, alcoholic, roasted, or stir-fried.

    Turtle Back

    When wind and cold invade the spinal cord, the back becomes tall like a turtle. This should be treated with Er Huo San. Apply moxibustion to the lung shu point, located on the sides below the third thoracic vertebra; and to the diaphragm shu point, below the seventh thoracic vertebra, with three to five moxibustion applications each. There are also cases of early sitting leading to stooped posture, which can be treated with Liu Wei Wan combined with Yi Ren, Mu Gua, Dang Gui, and Rou Gui.

    Delayed Walking

    Delayed walking is associated with deficiencies in both the liver and kidneys. The kidneys govern the bones; if they are deficient, the marrow does not fill the bones, leading to weakness and difficulty in walking. The liver governs the tendons; if it is deficient, the blood does not nourish the tendons, causing weakness and inability to support the bones. This condition should be treated with Hu Jing Wan.[82p]

    　　地黄丸 【《小儿直诀》，下同】 　治肾虚解颅，或行迟、语迟等证。　　熟地黄八钱，酒洗；益肾水，滋真阴，补血生精　山茱萸肉补肾添精　干山药各四钱，凉而能补　牡丹皮凉肾泻阴中之火，治足少阴无汗之骨蒸　泽泻补阴入肾经　白茯苓各三钱，入壬癸　　右地黄杵膏，余为末，加炼蜜丸桐子大，每股二三十丸，空心白汤下。薛己曰：按前丸治肾经，虚热作渴，小便淋秘，痰气上壅；或肝经血虚，燥热，风客淫气而患瘰疬结核；或四肢发搐，眼目瞤动；或肺经虚火咳嗽，吐血，头目眩晕；或咽喉燥痛，口舌疮裂；或心经血虚有火，自汗盗汗，便血诸血；或脾虚湿热，下刑于肾，腰膝不利；或疥癣疮痛等证，并用前药为主，而佐以各脏之药。大抵此药为天一生水之剂。若禀赋不足，肢体瘦弱，解颅失音，或畏明下窜，五迟五软，肾疳、肝疳，或早近女色，精气亏耗，五脏齐损，凡诸虚不足之证，皆用此以滋化源，其功不能尽述。[83p]

    Fang

    Di Huang Wan
    [From "Xiao Er Zhi Jue," same below]
    Treats kidney deficiency and symptoms like delayed movement or speech.

    Ingredients:

    • Shu Di Huang (Processed Rehmannia Root) - 8 qian, washed with wine; nourishes kidney water, enriches true yin, replenishes blood and generates essence.
    • Shan Zhu Yu (Cornelian Cherry Fruit) - supplements the kidneys and enhances essence.
    • Gan Shen Yao (Dried Chinese Yam) - 4 qian each; cool and nourishing.
    • Mu Dan Pi (Tree Peony Bark) - cools the kidneys and drains the fire from within the yin; treats bone steaming due to lack of sweat in the Shaoyin.
    • Ze Xie (Alisma) - nourishes yin and enters the kidney channel.
    • Bai Fu Ling (Poria) - 3 qian each, enters the Ren and Gui.

    The prepared Shu Di Huang is ground into a paste, and the others are powdered, mixed with refined honey to form pills the size of tung seeds, taking 20 to 30 pills at a time with warm water on an empty stomach. Xue Ji said: This formula primarily treats the kidney channel, addressing symptoms of deficiency heat, such as thirst, painful urination, phlegm and gas obstruction; blood deficiency in the liver channel causing dryness and heat, leading to wind-heat afflictions like scrofula and tuberculosis; spasms in the limbs, eyelid twitching; lung channel deficiency heat causing cough, blood expectoration, dizziness; dry and painful throat, sores on tongue and lips; heart blood deficiency with heat causing night sweats and blood in the stool; spleen deficiency causing damp heat affecting the kidneys, leading to weakness in the lower back and knees; or symptoms of skin diseases like scabies and sores. This formula serves as a primary remedy, supplemented with medicinal agents for other organs. Overall, this remedy is based on the essence of celestial water. If one is constitutionally weak, with emaciated limbs, loss of speech, or experiences fear of light with prolapsus, five delays and five weaknesses, kidney and liver deficiencies, or premature sexual engagement leading to depletion of essence and energy in all five organs, all symptoms of deficiency should use this to nourish and revitalize. Its efficacy cannot be fully described.[83p]

    　　红内消散 【《本草纲目》】 　治小儿龟背。　　红内消即赤何首乌

    Red Internal Dissipation
    To treat children's turtle back. Red internal dissipation refers to red vine (He Shou Wu). Grind it to a fine powder, mix with turtle urine, and apply to the joints on the back. Over time, it will stabilize.

    To treat children with delayed movement.     Includes processed rhubarb, adiantum without heart, blanched almonds, lily, fried mulberry bark, akebia, sweet ginseng, made into honey pills, taken with boiling water.

    Turtle Chest Pills
    To treat children's turtle chest and turtle back, caused by lung heat and bloating, which gradually develop into this disease; if nursing mothers consume too much spicy food, it can also lead to this condition.     　　枳壳防风丸
    　　枳壳麸炒　防风　独活　大黄煨　前胡　当归　麻黄去节，各三钱　　右为细末，面糊丸如黍米大，每服十丸，米饮食后服。
    　　大黄丸 【《证治准绳》，下同】 　治龟胸，肺热壅滞，心膈闷满。　　大黄七钱半，微炒　天冬焙　杏仁麸炒微黄　百合　木通　桑白皮　甜葶苈隔纸炙紫　(石卜)硝各五钱　　右为细末，蜜丸如绿豆大，不时温水研五丸，量儿大小加减。《幼科类萃》去(石卜)硝，加石膏。
    　　百合丹　即前大黄丸加减。
    　　百合一两　(石卜)硝　杏仁汤浸去皮尖　桑白皮　木通　川大黄　天门冬各五钱　　右为极细末，炼蜜和，如黍米大，每服十粒，米饮送下，量儿大小加减。
    　　龟胸丸
    　　苍朮　黄蘗酒炒　芍药酒炒　陈皮　防风　山楂　威灵仙　当归　　右为末，蜜丸，食后温水下，利后加生地黄。[85p]

    Zhike Fangfeng Wan
    Zhike (bitter orange peel) stir-fried with wheat bran, Fangfeng (siler), Du Huo (pubescent angelica), Da Huang (rhubarb) stewed, Qian Hu (hogfennel), Dang Gui (Angelica sinensis), and Ma Huang (ephedra) without stems, each three qian. Grind these into a fine powder, and make into pills the size of millet grains. Take ten pills after meals with rice.

    Da Huang Wan
    For treating turtle chest (a condition of lung heat stagnation) and fullness in the heart's diaphragm. Seven and a half qian of Da Huang, lightly stir-fried, Tian Dong (asparagus), almonds stir-fried to a light yellow, Bai He (lily bulb), Mu Tong (pipe vine), Sang Bai Pi (white mulberry root), and Tian Liu Li (sweet thorn) roasted under paper, five qian each. Grind these into a fine powder, mix with honey to form pills the size of green beans. Take five pills with warm water, adjusting quantities for children as needed. In "Youke Lei Cui," omit (Tian Liu Li) and add gypsum.

    Bai He Dan
    This is the previous Da Huang Wan with adjustments.
    One liang of Bai He, (Tian Liu Li), almonds soaked in soup and peeled, Sang Bai Pi, Mu Tong, Chuan Da Huang (Sichuan rhubarb), and Tian Men Dong (asparagus), each five qian. Grind these into an extremely fine powder, refine with honey, and form pills the size of millet grains. Take ten pills with rice wine, adjusting quantities for children as needed.

    Gui Xiong Wan
    Cang Zhu (atractylodes), Huang Bo (whose bark is stir-fried with wine), Shao Yao (peony), Chen Pi (dried tangerine peel), Fang Feng, Shan Zha (hawthorn), Wei Ling Xian (clematis), and Dang Gui. Grind these into a powder, mix with honey to form pills, and take them with warm water after meals. Adjust with Sheng Di Huang (raw Chinese rhubarb) for relieving effects.[85p]

    　　松蕊丹　治龟背病。
    　　川大黄炮　前胡　麻黄去根节　桂心各半两　松花洗焙　枳壳去瓤麸炒　独活　防风各一两　　右为细末，炼蜜和如黍米大，每服十粒，粥饮下，量儿大小加减。圣惠麻黄丸多芍药，少前胡。一方多槟榔、诃皮。一方无松花，有当归，煮面和丸，名枳壳防风丸。
    　　鹿茸丹　治数岁不能行。
    　　麝香　鹿茸酥炙黄　生地黄　虎胫骨酥涂炙　当归洗焙干　黄芪銼　　右件各一两为细末，用羊髓四两煮烂，和成膏，如黍米大，每服十粒，磨沉香汤下，乳食前，日三服。
    　　羚羊角丸　治小儿肾虚，或病后筋骨弱，五六岁不能行，宜补益肝肾。　　羚羊角尖细而节密者错取末　生干地黄焙　虎胫骨敲破，涂酥炙黄　酸枣仁去皮称炒　白茯苓各半两　桂去皮，取有味处，不得见火　防风　当归　黄芪切焙，各二钱半　　右同为细末，炼蜜和成剂，每服一皂子大，儿大者加之，食前温水化下，日三四服，久服取效。[86p]

    Song Rui Dan: Treats turtle shell disease.
    Ingredients:

    • 1.5g of Sichuan Dahuang (rhubarb)
    • 1.5g of Qianhu (Corydalis root)
    • 1.5g of Mahuang (ephedra) without roots
    • 1.5g of Guixin (cinnamon heart)
    • 1.5g of Songhua (pine pollen) washed and roasted
    • 1.5g of Zhihua (bitter orange) without pulp and roasted with flour
    • 1g each of Duhuo (angelica) and Fangfeng (pepper)
      Grind all above into a fine powder, mix with honey until the size of millet grains. Take ten granules with congee based on the child’s size. Shenghui Mahuang Wan contains more Shaoyao (peony) and less Qianhu. One formula has more Bingtang (betel nut) and He pi (gambir). Another formula lacks Songhua and has Danggui (angelica), boiled with flour into pills, named Zhihua Fangfeng Wan.

    Lu Rong Dan: Treats children unable to walk for several years.
    Ingredients:

    • 1g of Musk
    • 1g of Lu Rong (deer antler) roasted
    • 1g of Shengdi Huang (raw rehmannia)
    • 1g of Hujinggu (tiger's bone) roasted with fat
    • 1g of Danggui (angelica) washed and roasted dry
    • 1g of Huangqi (astragalus)
      Grind all into a fine powder, boil with four liang of sheep marrow until melted, and mix into a paste the size of millet grains. Take ten granules, ground with sandalwood tea before dairy meals, three times a day.

    Lingyang Jiao Wan: Treats children with kidney deficiency or weak bones and muscles after illness, suitable for nourishing liver and kidneys.
    Ingredients:

    • Take the tip of the antelope horn that is thin and well-knit
    • 1g each of Shengdi Huang (raw rehmannia) roasted
    • 1g of Hujinggu (tiger's bone) smashed and roasted
    • 1g of Suanzaoren (sour jujube seed) peeled and roasted
    • 1g of Bai Fuling (white poria)
    • 0.75g each of Gui (cinnamon) without bark, Fangfeng (pepper), Danggui (angelica), and Huangqi (astragalus) cut and roasted
      Grind all into a fine powder, mix with honey into granules. Take one piece the size of a soap bar; for larger children, increase dosage. Take before meals with warm water, three to four times a day for effectiveness with long-term use.[86p]

    　　生干地黄丸　治儿十岁不行。
    　　生地黄　当归焙　防风　酸枣仁微炒　赤茯　黄芪　芎藭　羚羊角　羌活　甘草炙微赤　桂心各等分　　右，捣罗蜜九如菉豆大，食前温酒下，量儿加减。
    　　虎骨散
    　　虎胫骨酒炙　生地黄　酸枣仁酒浸去皮炒　辣桂去皮　白茯苓去皮　防风　当归俱去芦　川芎　牛膝酒浸去芦，各等分　　右为极细末，每服一钱半，以粥饮调，次入好酒二滴再调，食前服，日二。一方用炼蜜丸如黍米大，木瓜汤下五丸，或十丸。《宝鉴》加黄芪。
    　　三因五加皮散　治小儿三岁不能行者，由受气不足，体力虚怯，腰脊脚膝筋软，足故不能行。　　真五加皮　为末，粥饮调，次入好酒少许，每服一栗壳许，日三服效。[87p]

    Sheng Gan Di Huang Wan is used to treat children of ten years who cannot walk. The ingredients are: raw Rehmannia, prepared Angelica, baked Fangfeng, lightly stir-fried sour jujube pit, red Poria, Astragalus, Chuanxiong, antelope horn, Qianghuo, honey-fried Glycyrrhiza, and cassia heart, all in equal parts. Crush and pound them to the size of walnuts, and take them with warm wine before meals, adjusting the dosage according to the child's needs.

    Hu Gu San consists of: tiger bone wine-fried, raw Rehmannia, sour jujube pit soaked in wine, skin removed and fried, peeled spicy cassia, peeled white Poria, Fangfeng, Angelica (with the pith removed), Chuanxiong, and wine-soaked Niu Xi with the pith removed, all in equal parts. Grind into a very fine powder. Take one and a half qian (about 4.5 grams) mixed with porridge, adding two drops of good wine before consuming, twice a day. Another preparation can be shaped into pills the size of millet, taken with papaya soup, five to ten pills at a time. The Bao Jian formula adds Astragalus.

    San Yin Wu Jia Pi San is used for children of three years who cannot walk due to insufficient qi, weak physique, and soft tendons in the waist, spine, legs, and knees, hindering movement. The main ingredient is powdered true Wu Jia Pi, mixed with porridge, then a small amount of good wine is added. Each dose is about the size of a chestnut shell, taken three times daily for effect.[87p]

    　　柴胡饮　治小儿骨热，肺脉寒，长不能行，骨热疳劳，肌肉消瘦。　　柴胡　鳖甲米酢涂炙黄色　知母　桔梗　枳壳麸炒　元参　升麻　　右件各等分，细銼，三岁以下药半两，水五合煎二合，分二服，空心食前服。忌毒物。服后澡浴。
    　　澡浴方
    　　苦参　茯苓皮　苍朮　桑白皮　白矾各半两　葱白少许　　右銼，沸水二升，浸药一两，通与儿浴，温处避风。
    　　左经丸　治筋骨诸疾，手足不随，不能行步走动。　　草乌头生肉白者去皮脐　木鳖去壳　白胶香　五灵脂各三两半　盘蝥去翅足，一百枚，酢煮熟　当归一两　　右为末，黑豆去皮，生杵粉一斤，酢糊丸鸡头实大，酒磨下一丸。不曾针灸伤筋络者，四五丸必效。十岁儿一丸，分三服。此药能通荣卫，导经络，专治心肾肝三经，服后小便少淋濇，乃其验也。按此方非内有污血痼疾，不宜用。[88p]

    Chaihu Decoction treats young children's bone heat, cold in the lung channels, inability to walk due to prolonged ailments, and symptoms of malnutrition.

    Ingredients: Chaihu, tortoise shell, rice vinegar (roasted to a yellow color), Zhimu, Jiegeng, fried Zhiqiao, Yuanshen, Shengma.

    Combine these ingredients in equal parts, grind finely. For children under three years old, use half a liang of this medicine, boil in five cups of water to yield two cups of decoction, divide into two doses, and take on an empty stomach before meals. Avoid toxic substances. Take a bath afterwards.

    Bathing prescription:

    Ingredients: Ku Shen, Fuling peel, Cangzhu, Sangbai skin, and white alum, each half a liang, a small amount of green onion.

    Grind them, steep in two liters of boiling water, soak one liang of the medicine, and give the child a bath, ensuring warmth and avoiding windy places.

    Zuo Jing Pills treat various ailments of the muscles and bones, including unresponsive hands and feet, inability to walk or move.

    Ingredients: Cao Wutou (remove the skin and navel) three and a half liang; Mu Bie (remove the shell); Baijiao Xiang; Wulingzhi, each three and a half liang; Panmou, remove wings and legs, one hundred pieces, boiled in vinegar until cooked; Danggui one liang.

    Grind these into a powder, mix with peeled black beans, one jin of raw pestle powder, and vinegar to form pills the size of a chicken head. Don't use in cases of acupuncture injury to the tendons; four to five pills will certainly be effective. For a ten-year-old, give one pill divided into three doses. This medicine can regulate the protective and nutritive Qi, guide the meridians, and specifically treat the heart, kidneys, and liver. If the patient experiences decreased urination after taking it, that is a sign of its effectiveness. Note that this remedy is inappropriate if there is stagnant blood or chronic illness inside.[88p]

    　　续命丹　治小儿銼骨，行步艰难，脚无力。　　防风　乳香　蔓荆子　牛膝　麻黄　羚羊角　枣仁　草乌头　没药　白朮　茯苓各二钱半　天麻酒煮　胡麻炒　当归　续断各半两　川乌头去皮　黄芪各四钱　蒺藜一钱二分半　　右为细末，蜜丸小弹大，每服一丸，煎酒细嚼，一日三五服。用后洗药，服药三日方洗。

    　　降气消痰汤 【《活幼精要》】[89p]

    Life-Extending Pill
    Treats children with bone grinding, making walking difficult and their feet weak.
    Ingredients:

    • 2.5 qian of Fangfeng (Siler)
    • 2.5 qian of Ruxiang (Frankincense)
    • 2.5 qian of Manjingzi (Vitex Fructus)
    • 2.5 qian of Niuxi (Achyranthes)
    • 2.5 qian of Mahuang (Ephedra)
    • 2.5 qian of Lingyangjiao (Antelope Horn)
    • 2.5 qian of Daoren (Jujube Seed)
    • 2.5 qian of Caowutou (Aconite)
    • 2.5 qian of Moye (Myrrh)
    • 2.5 qian of Baizhu (Atractylodes)
    • 2.5 qian of Fuling (Poria)
    • 0.5 liang of Tianma (Gastrodia) prepared in wine
    • 0.5 liang of Huama (Sesame) roasted
    • 0.5 liang of Danggui (Angelica)
    • 0.5 liang of Xuduan (Dipsacus)
    • 4 qian each of Chuanwutou (Aconite, peeled) and Huangqi (Astragalus)
    • 1.25 qian of Jizhu (Tribulus)

    Grind the above into a fine powder, mix with honey to form small pills, take one pill each time, chew it well in wine, three to five times a day. After using, wash the medicine, and take the medicine for three days before washing.

    Medicine Washing Formula
    1 liang each of

    • Caowutou (Aconite)
    • Danggui (Angelica)
    • Dilu (Earthworm)
    • Mubiezi (Tamarind)
    • Zibeicao (Purple Lonicera)
    • Jiao Mu (Peppers)
    • Congxu (Scallions)
    • Jingjie (Schizonepeta)

    Grind into powder, boil in soup, wash the toenails from above, then use fumigation method.

    Fumigation Formula
    1 liang each of

    • Chaihu (Bupleurum)
    • Caowutou (Aconite)
    • Chixiaodou (Adzuki Bean)
    • Wuzhuyu (Evodia)
    • Qianghuo (Notopterygium)
    • Wancansha (Silkworm Sand)

    Grind and combine with three sheng of black beans soaked in hot water; after a while, remove beans, boil the previous medicine, and use a basin to fumigate the affected area, causing perspiration from the bones.

    Lily Dan [from “Young Child’s Compendium”]
    Soaked in yellow wine, seven and a half qian, tian dong, apricot kernels, lily, mulberry bark, stir-fried terophis, gypsum, bitter orange, trachelospermum, raw licorice each five qian, refined honey made into pills.

    Er Huo San
    Qiang huo, Du huo, ginseng, astragalus, coix seeds, angelica, cinnamon, eucommia, Note: this formula originally lacks dosage and preparation method.

    Tiger Limb Pills
    Tiger limb bones, cooked earth, cornelian cherry, cow knee, yam, angelica, papaya, chuanxiong, deer antler, coix seeds, wujia pi, cinnamon, honey pills the size of a walnut, for a three-year-old, take three pills daily. Those with internal heat should omit cinnamon.

    Modified Cooked Rehmannia Pills
    Cooked rehmannia, cornelian cherry, peony root, yam, cow knee, alisma, deer antler, cinnamon, bu-gu-zhi, ginseng soaked in children’s urine and roasted, white recheer, refined honey made into pills.

    Coix Seed Pills [from “Introduction to Medicine”]
    For treating children’s hand tendons that are contracted and cannot stretch. Two liang coix seeds, one liang each of angelica, gentian, sour jujube seeds, windbreak, qian huo. Grind the above into powder, form into honey pills the size of qian seeds, one to two pills with musk and jing jie decoction to be taken down.[90p]
